British Cabinet Discusses European Situation: Main Tendency of Foreign Policy, No Commitment to Eastern European Pact, Continues Mediation Mission in Stresa Conference

(London) The Cabinet held a routine meeting today to discuss the current diplomatic situation based on information obtained by British ministers from Berlin, Moscow, and Warsaw. According to informed sources, the main tendencies of British foreign policy are roughly as follows: (1) Regarding the Eastern European Mutual Assistance Pact, Britain will not take any commitments on the Eastern European side. The security of Eastern European countries should be resolved by the countries concerned themselves. It is not impossible for the countries concerned to conclude a European pact, including clauses stipulating the "definition of an aggressor," but Britain will not participate in such "definition of an aggressor" clauses. However, Britain will continue to provide moral support for various collective security initiatives. (2) Britain will continue to mediate between Czechoslovakia and other powers at the Stresa conference to ease the European situation. Since Britain regards itself as a mediator at the Stresa conference, it can create a situation to indirectly compel Germany to participate in collective security organizations. Britain cannot support the great powers' negotiations of various agreements without regard to Czechoslovakia and without exchanging information with Germany. Britain believes that it is essential to avoid giving Germany the impression that Germany has been thrown out of European coordination. It is essential to make Germany deeply believe that the great powers have no intention of excluding Czechoslovakia, so that the opportunity for negotiations can be used at any time to allow Germany to participate in all the peaceful efforts of other countries. For this reason, the Italian newspaper "Il Popolo d'Italia" recently advocated that the Stresa conference should decide on a common action program to cope with certain future events. Britain is not in a position to approve of this proposal. (3) The British diplomatic community hopes that Britain, France, and Italy will jointly negotiate a declaration to be submitted to the extraordinary meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council on April 15, so that the Executive Council can accept the declaration without further discussion. This declaration should reiterate the attitude taken by the great powers regarding Germany's announcement of the abolition of the military clauses of the Treaty of Versailles, but at the same time, the door should remain open to continue negotiations with Germany. In addition, a clause may be included in the declaration stipulating that countries should consult each other when it is necessary to take collective action to maintain peace. The above is the general tendency of British foreign policy, but this tendency is by no means immutable. So far, it is still exploratory. Whether it will succeed depends on the attitude of the countries concerned. (Havas telegram from the 3rd)

(London) The British Cabinet will meet on Friday to hear reports from Lord Privy Seal Eden's visits to Moscow, Warsaw, and Prague. Next week, Foreign Secretary Simon and Eden will go to Stresa, but Prime Minister MacDonald may not attend the tripartite conference. Political circles do not expect the Stresa conference to produce significant results, but they attach importance to the meeting of the League of Nations Executive Council to be convened on April 15. (Guomin News Agency telegram from the 4th)

Mussolini Puts Forward Plan

(London) According to the Daily Telegraph, Italian Prime Minister Mussolini will put forward a plan at the Stresa conference. Mussolini believes that before attempting to conclude various mutual assistance pacts, it is necessary to first create the strongest possible feeling to enable countries to trust each other. Therefore, Mussolini may put forward a declaration to be signed jointly by European countries, with a suggestion attached to reopen economic and political negotiations to improve the relations between countries. This plan will be based on last year's Italian-Austrian-Hungarian agreement, which stipulates that countries should consult each other on all issues concerning the overall European situation, and a conference of the countries concerned may be convened at the request of a signatory country. The purpose of the Italian-Austrian-Hungarian agreement was to stipulate a common policy to improve the political and economic relations of the Danube countries. Now Mussolini's plan is to expand the scope of this agreement to promote it to all European countries. (Havas telegram from the 4th)

(Paris) Foreign Minister Laval is now scheduled to depart for Stresa, Italy, on the evening of the 10th of this month to attend the British-French-Italian conference. Many important officials from the Ministry of Foreign Affairs, such as Secretary-General Léger, will accompany Laval. (Havas telegram from the 3rd)

French Side Intends to Revise the Pact

(Paris) According to reliable sources, French officials today plan to revise the proposed Eastern European Pact to allow Poland to participate. The origin of the French plan is due to Poland's refusal to participate in the pact in its current form. It is generally hoped that Germany may also be able to approve of it after the revision. At the same time, France has launched a major plan to build aircraft. The Senate has approved the expansion of the Air Force. By the end of 1935, the strength of the French Air Force will be so great that Germany will not be able to catch up in the short term. In terms of diplomacy, France still intends to conclude military defense agreements with the Soviet Union and other countries. It is said that Czechoslovakia may also participate, but this depends on whether the tripartite conference convened by Italian Prime Minister Mussolini can agree on a broader security pact. Generally speaking, France will have concrete suggestions for the pact to deal with the opposition of Polish Minister of Military Affairs Marshal Piłsudski. The content of the suggestions will probably bring the Eastern European countries into a more direct relationship with the League of Nations, rather than engaging exclusively in purely military alliances. As for whether the Italian conference will invite Eastern European countries to participate together, diplomatic circles are still discussing it. (Guomin News Agency telegram from the 4th)

French Newspapers Observe as a Failure

(Paris) Newspapers commented on the talks between Britain and Poland in Warsaw, most of which believed that the results did not produce any new developments. This should be given great attention. It also said, "When Polish Foreign Minister Colonel Beck and Minister of Military Affairs Piłsudski spoke with British Lord Privy Seal Eden, they did not explicitly reject the Eastern European Pact." "Le Petit Journal" carried an article by Deputy Chairman of the House of Representatives Foreign Affairs Committee, Tessan, saying, "Foreign Minister Laval's trip to Warsaw may make Poland no longer hold an ambiguous attitude. This will benefit Poland itself and the future of peace in Europe." In addition, "Le Petit Journal" also stated that Eden's trip to Moscow was declared a success, while the trip to Warsaw ended in failure. Colonel Beck could have chosen between the pro-French or pro-German camps, but unfortunately, he had already made a choice. His choice may not run counter to the Franco-Polish alliance." Austrian Cabinet Issues Communiqué: Imitates Germany in Reorganizing Armaments, Says Necessary Preparations Have Begun, Part of France's Encirclement Plan

The Vienna government today issued a communiqué declaring that Austria is prepared to imitate Germany in abolishing the armaments restrictions of the Treaty of Versailles, and in concise terms stated, "The necessary preparations have already begun." It is said that Austria is currently the only country in Europe without a military organization, while its neighbors have all made efforts to expand their armaments. Observers say that the diplomatic side has notified France and has sought France's consent. Chancellor Schuschnigg's government is very friendly to France and has made every effort to prevent union with Germany. Therefore, its armaments reorganization plan may also be implemented on this basis. It is understood that Austria's plan is also part of France's encirclement of Germany and may participate in the proposed mutual defense pact within a possible range. The commanders of the Austrian army's reserve forces have been ordered to report, probably for the purpose of mobilizing new troops. (Guomin News Agency telegram from the 4th)

Vienna After a cabinet meeting last night, a statement was issued saying that the Austrian government has decided to ask the great powers to allow the reintroduction of compulsory military service. This move was prohibited by the Treaty of Saint-Germain. Austrian leaders clearly want to avoid causing condemnation and possible consequences by unilaterally denying the treaty. They may fear that the Little Entente and the Balkan Entente will follow the example of other former enemy countries and introduce compulsory military service, and the threat that the countries will immediately mobilize to deal with it will be realized. The communiqué said, "The cabinet meeting today, chaired by Chancellor Dr. Schuschnigg, discussed the issue of expanding the Austrian army. Cabinet members were unanimous in their opinion that allowing Austria to have full equality is a self-evident assumption. Therefore, necessary preparatory steps will be taken now." Vice Chancellor and Commander of the Home Guard Starhemberg did not attend this meeting, which is noteworthy. According to informed political figures, the Austrian government now intends to increase the army by 60,000 men by using selective conscription in the auxiliary forces. According to the provisions of the Treaty of Saint-Germain, universal conscription should be abolished. The Austrian army, including officers and headquarters troops, is limited to 30,000 men. The Austrian government is now trying to ask the great powers to revise the treaty. (Reuters telegram from the 3rd)

Vienna According to observations from powerful sources, Austria's announcement of the abolition of the armaments clause of the Treaty of Versailles must have reached some kind of diplomatic understanding with France. The Austrian government, led by Schuschnigg, has a very strong pro-French color, and France is most concerned about its connection with Nazi Germany. Therefore, based on the above, Austria's armaments revival is realized. (Dentsu telegram from the 4th)

Czechoslovakia Expresses No Surprise

Prague, the capital of Czechoslovakia, The Czech government and public did not express surprise at the Austrian government's announcement of the equality of armaments rights. The foreign ministers of the Little Entente had already considered this at the meeting in Belgrade, the capital of Yugoslavia, and Bratislava, Czechoslovakia. The Little Entente believes that the right to equality of armaments should be reviewed by the Executive Council of the League of Nations, but unilateral action to adopt any position is resolutely opposed by the Little Entente. (Havas from the 4th)

British-Polish Commercial Treaty Concluded: Increase in Poland's Foreign Trade

Warsaw correspondence The commercial treaty between Britain and Poland has been formally signed after repeated negotiations. According to the provisions of the treaty, the treaty will take effect on December 31 of this year. The Polish press and the relevant industrial and commercial circles are paying close attention to this. The Polish people unanimously recognize that the conclusion of this commercial treaty is closely related to the revision of other commercial treaties recently due to the implementation of Poland's new tax rate. Because Britain is still the largest buyer of Polish goods, and Poland is also beneficial to the exchange of goods between Britain and Poland, it is generally hoped that after the conclusion of this new treaty, trade between Britain and Poland can be further developed and both sides can benefit. All private commercial treaties previously concluded between Britain and Poland, such as coal agreements, will be important data for this commercial treaty. Poland's foreign trade, which has the largest surplus, is mainly with Britain, with a surplus of 105,700,000 Polish zlotys last year. The largest deficit is mainly with Switzerland, followed by France. In overseas trade, the United States has a surplus of 98,000,000 Polish zlotys with Poland, but Poland has a surplus in overseas trade with China, French South Africa, Palestine, and other countries. According to recent statistics, the total value of Poland's foreign trade exports in January of this year was 79,291,000 Polish zlotys, and the total value of imports was 61,938,000 Polish zlotys, with a total surplus of 16,353,000 Polish zlotys, an increase of 953,000 Polish zlotys compared to the surplus in the same month last year. It is expected that after the implementation of the British-Polish commercial treaty and other revised commercial treaties, the surplus will be even more considerable. The most important of Poland's export goods are wheat, rye, barley, oats, sugar beet, wheat flour, rye flour, hops, cattle, pigs, butter, feathers, and down, pig bristles, petroleum, zinc, fur, pure wool, and wool textiles, flax, and flax silk, timber (mostly railway sleepers), plywood, wood panels, bentwood furniture, pig iron, railway steel pipes and water pipes, etc.

U.S. Fleet to Hold Exercises in the Pacific Starting May 3rd; Commander of U.S. Asiatic Fleet to Visit Japan to Explain; Exercise Plan to Form a Large Triangular Formation

(Washington) Secretary of the Navy Swanson announced today that the U.S. fleet is scheduled to begin exercises in the Pacific on May 3rd. To dispel any ill feelings in Japan arising from this, the commander of the U.S. Asiatic Fleet will visit Yokohama on that day as a friendly gesture. Swanson stated to reporters his personal opinion that future naval conferences should include Germany, but he has not received any submission from Germany regarding this matter. Sweden's intention to have a navy of 450,000 tons will not affect the 5:5:3 ratio in the U.S., Britain, and Japan's case. (Reuters dispatch, 3rd)

(Washington) Fearing that the fleet exercises in the Pacific will arouse suspicion in Japan regarding any war intentions, the U.S. will send two batches of goodwill envoys to Japan to explain. The first batch is Admiral Hepburn, commander of the Asiatic Fleet, who will arrive in Yokohama on May 3rd, the date the exercises begin, aboard the flagship Augusta. Afterwards, a squadron of destroyers from the Asiatic Fleet will visit Kobe. This demonstration of goodwill was announced today by Secretary of the Navy Swanson. Prior to this, the naval department had received multiple telegrams opposing the exercises, calling them a demonstration of force against Japan. Swanson stated that this accusation is unfounded because the U.S. fleet exercises will be 2,000 miles from the Japanese coast, and this move was announced a year ago, when the fleet had not yet sailed to the Atlantic. Therefore, the current plan cannot be seen as a result of Japan's withdrawal from the Washington Naval Treaty. Several religious groups, such as the Christian Church and the National Association, have strongly opposed the exercises. Swanson's statement today is the first time the Navy Department has stated its position. The U.S. fleet's exercise plan will form a large triangle between San Diego, Dutch Harbor, and the Hawaiian Islands. Whether the fleet will go to the Philippines has not yet been announced, but it is said that this year's exercise does not include this plan. (National Telegraph, 3rd)

U.S. Economic Mission Arrives in Tokyo Last Night

Remarks on the Return Trip of a Traveling Official: British and American Loans Cannot Be Realized; Investigation and Suppression of Anti-Japanese Movement to Be Conducted

(Tokyo) Mr. Yokotake Heitaro, the Commercial Attaché stationed in Shanghai, departed from Tokyo on the third. He boarded the Nagasaki Maru in Kobe today to return to Shanghai. After Yokotake arrives in Shanghai, he will report to Ambassador Arima on the government's policy of Sino-Japanese economic cooperation and the opinions of the private sector, and also consult with the Chinese government and business community on concrete methods of economic cooperation. (Japan United Press dispatch, 4th)

Kobe Commercial Attaché Yokotake made a speech before his departure, stating, "The first thing I realized upon returning to my country is that Japan, both the government and the public, are genuinely concerned about the Chinese issue. I lectured on the Chinese issue more than 40 times in Tokyo, Osaka, and other places, which is something I have never experienced in my past life. When I left China, I predicted that the Lunar New Year would be the most dangerous time for the Shanghai financial community. However, it is now April, and the financial community not only has no crisis but also has news of digesting 200 million yuan of domestic debt. The issue of silver outflow is also not likely to be significant. The total amount of silver owned by the Chinese people is 1 billion or 2 billion, and Shanghai alone has at least 200 million yuan of silver. This is the reality of the Chinese economy. The issue of British and American loans to China has no possibility of realization. Britain has no courage to loan alone, and American silver policy is also ineffective. How can we talk about loans? After I return to Shanghai, the first task I should carry out is to investigate how the anti-Japanese movement is being suppressed. This is not supposed to be the task of a commercial attaché, but a commercial attaché stationed in China has no choice but to do this kind of work. In short, opening up the facts and reducing the anti-Japanese movement is the goal that should be achieved first." (Japan United Press dispatch, 4th)

The One Who Tied the Knot Must Untie It; Petitioning Laborers Go to Manchuria

According to the Manchuria Daily News of March 29th, since the Manchurian authorities and the Kwantung Bureau formulated regulations to control labor, the Regulations for the Control of Laborers have been implemented on March 15th. Article 2 of the regulations imposes strict restrictions on labor in agriculture, forestry, fishery, industry, commerce, civil engineering construction, material transportation, and other transportation-related activities, prohibiting entry. As a result, Shandong coolies have been prevented from entering. In March of last year, 110,000 people landed in Dalian, but this year it is less than 40,000. Unexpectedly, the entire Manchurian industrial community suddenly reported an insufficient supply of laborers, especially in the Southern Manchuria industrial sector. However, the Manchurian industrial community is actively engaged in construction, and this has severely impacted the future of industry. The Dalian Industrial Association recently petitioned the Dalian Chamber of Commerce and Industry to request the Kwantung Bureau to allow laborers to enter Manchuria and to formulate special rules to ease the restrictions. The Secretary-General of the Changyong Dalian Chamber of Commerce also went to Changchun on the night of the 20th. On the 27th, the Kwantung Army Advisor Ueki exchanged views with the Kwantung Army on ways to remedy the situation. If there is no other alternative to allow laborers from inside the Shanhai Pass to go to Manchuria, then the future of Manchurian construction is quite worrying.

Amendments to the Exchange Law; Review of Conditions Completed

(Nanjing) The draft amendments to the Exchange Law have been completed by the Legislative Yuan's Commerce and Finance Committees and will be reviewed by the Yuan meeting on the morning of the 5th. (Central News Agency dispatch, 4th)

(Nanjing) The draft amendments to the Exchange Law have been reviewed and finalized by the joint meeting of the Finance and Commercial Law Committees of the Legislative Yuan and will be submitted to the general assembly on the 5th for discussion. The amended conditions and newly added conditions are as follows: A. Amended articles: After Article 31, it is decided to amend "The buying and selling parties shall each pay a security deposit in accordance with the provisions of the articles of association, and the ratio of the amount to the registered price of the transaction shall be in accordance with the following provisions: (1) The commodity transaction shall not be less than 10 percent, but cotton yarn shall not be less than 5 percent; (2) The securities transaction shall not be less than 8 percent; (3) The gold transaction shall not be less than 5 percent." Article 38, amend the second item, the original second item is changed to the third item, and the words "the preceding paragraph" in the text are changed to "the first paragraph of this article," and are amended together as follows: "The transaction slip of the preceding paragraph's transaction shall be filled out by the exchange and signed by both brokers or members. If the broker or member violates the first paragraph of this article, he shall be punished in accordance with Article 50. Article 42, the Ministry of Industry shall send exchange supervisors to inspect the business books and other items of the exchange, as well as the books of brokers or members, and pay attention to the causes of market price fluctuations. Exchange staff, brokers, or members shall have the obligation to provide items and answer questions for the preceding inspection. The Supervisory Yuan shall send personnel at any time to investigate all aspects of the exchange and the performance of duties by personnel sent by the competent authorities." B. Newly added conditions: "Article 41, brokers or members shall not accept commissions from public officials to engage in speculative transactions. If brokers or members violate this provision, they shall be fined two to ten times the amount of the security deposit. Article 48, those who violate the provisions of Article 41, the broker or member and the public official shall each be fined two to ten times the transaction price, and those involved in criminal offenses shall be punished in accordance with the criminal law. C. The words 'Ministry of Industry and Commerce' are changed to 'Ministry of Industry': The words 'Ministry of Industry and Commerce' in the various articles of the Exchange Law shall be uniformly changed to the words 'Ministry of Industry.'" (Special dispatch, 4th)

Farmers Gather and Riot Outside Xifengkou; Killing the Head of the Puppet Police Station and the Head of the Card; Japanese Army Dispatches Aircraft to Bomb

Yellow River's Momentum Slows Down; The Head of Changyuan County Presents Six Recommendations for Disaster Relief

(Tianjin) The Provincial Government received a telegram from the Head of Changyuan County stating that the Yellow River's water level is stable, its momentum has slowed down, and the danger has decreased. It is appropriate to take advantage of this time to quickly carry out flood prevention projects, which can achieve twice the results with half the effort. The danger in all sections of the Taihang Dike should be addressed together. The county also presented six recommendations for disaster relief. On the 27th of last month, the water level rose sharply, and the main current shifted north. The north wind was strong, and the water was counterattacked, which was an opportunity to build a diversion dam. He urged the militia to go to neighboring counties to cut willow branches to a length of 13 meters on the 30th night, and the cost was less than 1,000 yuan. Because the diversion dam was completed, the flow gradually slowed down, but most of the embankment in the Shiche section of the north bank collapsed, so it is necessary to quickly close it to prevent Guantai from being affected. Implementing Measures for Opium Suppression

(Hankou) The implementing measures for opium suppression are as follows: Article 1: Opium Suppression Procedures. In addition to adhering to the measures promulgated by the Executive Headquarters for dispatching personnel to investigate and prohibit opium cultivation, strictly enforcing regulations for prohibiting opium addiction and suppressing opium users, strictly prohibiting opium cultivation in inland provinces, suppressing the purchase of opium from border provinces, strictly prohibiting addictive drugs, suppressing opium paste shops, and other relevant regulations, all matters shall be handled in accordance with these measures. Article 2: The eight provinces of Henan, Hubei, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Jiangsu, Zhejiang, and Fujian are designated as absolutely opium-free provinces. Starting from April of this year, a general inspection will be implemented. Senior officials will be selected and dispatched, or personnel will be designated, to go to each province, cooperate with the provincial governments to effectively monitor and supervise the implementation. If opium seedlings are still found in counties that have already reported complete suppression, once verified, the county magistrate, the suppression committee member, and the district and village chiefs, as well as the opium farmers, will be severely punished according to military law. If there is any gathering of people to resist eradication, troops will be dispatched immediately to arrest the ringleaders, who will be executed by firing squad on the spot. If any police, military, or security teams protect opium cultivation, and the county magistrate is unable to prevent it, a secret report may be made directly to arrest and punish them. If a county magistrate fails to report and eradicate opium seedlings within his jurisdiction, or privately collects donations, once verified, he will be executed by firing squad to serve as a warning. Subsequently, during the planting season each year, inspections should be ordered and conducted, and reports should be submitted in accordance with regulations. A general inspection should be carried out during the emergence of seedlings to prevent a resurgence. Article 3: The provinces of Shaanxi and Gansu have been approved for phased opium suppression. According to the reports submitted by the two provinces, the opium suppression will be implemented in three phases according to the original plan. The counties that have already reported complete suppression will be inspected as scheduled in accordance with the previous article. The counties in the two provinces that are scheduled to implement opium suppression in the second and third phases should also be completely cleared within the specified time. Article 4: Each province and city should be responsible for carrying out the re-registration of opium addicts in accordance with the regulations for strictly prohibiting opium addiction and suppressing opium users. This should be thoroughly completed within six months. In the first three months, persuasion should be used to encourage registration, and efforts should be made to promote it. If there are still those who conceal themselves and fail to register, they should be completely ordered to register and forcibly executed within the three-month period. A simple method for issuing licenses for poor opium addicts should be established to remove obstacles to registration, in order to obtain accurate statistics on opium addicts as a standard for annual reduction. Those who fail to register after the deadline will no longer be allowed to register. If any unregistered individuals are found after the deadline, they should all be detained and ordered to quit. The number of people registered at the final registration deadline in the 24th year of the Republic will be taken as the total number, and compulsory detoxification will be carried out in order of the age of the opium addicts, divided into five phases, with one year as each phase. The minimum reduction each year is one-fifth. The first phase ends at the end of the 25th year of the Republic, reducing opium addicts by one-fifth. The second phase ends at the end of the 26th year of the Republic, reducing opium addicts by one-quarter. The third phase ends at the end of the 27th year of the Republic, reducing opium addicts by one-third. The fourth phase ends at the end of the 28th year of the Republic, reducing opium addicts by one-third. The fifth phase ends at the end of the 29th year of the Republic, completely eradicating opium addiction. Regarding the registration of opium addicts, if the regulations for strictly prohibiting opium addiction and suppressing opium users are not suitable for the actual situation of each province and city, causing opium addicts to hesitate to come forward to register, each province and city may carefully review and draft detailed implementation rules and submit them for approval, allowing for flexibility. Article 5: All personnel serving in the Party, government, and military, as well as faculty and students in schools, are absolutely prohibited from smoking opium. Those who have already become addicted are allowed to report and are given a deadline to quit. Those who conceal their addiction or relapse after reporting and quitting will be punished with the most severe penalties in accordance with military law. In addition to revising and promulgating the Measures for Limiting the Time for Quitting Opium for Party, Government, and Military Service Personnel and Students, as well as the Regulations for Quitting Opium Adjustment and Verification, which were promulgated in September of the 21st year of the Republic by the Headquarters of the Three Provinces of Henan, Hubei, and Anhui, the heads of Party, military, government, and school institutions, and all levels of responsible officials, shall be responsible for layer-by-layer supervision, as well as the organization of adjustment and verification and compulsory detoxification. Article 6: In each province and city, in order to limit opium smoking, before the 29th year of the Republic, the opium needed by all addicts should be purchased from border provinces by specially appointed merchants, in accordance with the Statistics on the purchase quantity, the merchants should adhere to the Regulations for Suppressing the Purchase of Opium from Border Provinces, apply for purchase permits, go to border provinces to purchase, and specify the transportation route. Temporarily follow the joint transportation procedure, with the Opium Suppression Supervisory Office implementing public transportation. After arriving at the destination, it should all be unloaded into public warehouses and distributed for sale. The quantity required by registered addicts in the 24th year of the Republic should be used as the standard for public purchase and transportation. From the 25th year of the Republic, the quantity required by addicts should be investigated and reduced year by year. All private transportation is prohibited, and violators will be treated as private traffickers. Article 7: The Opium Suppression Supervisory Office, in consultation with the provincial and municipal governments, should determine the number of opium paste shops allowed to be established in each province and city within two months after the completion of the re-registration of opium addicts, and report it together with the number of opium paste shops established by the Opium Suppression Supervisory Office in each province and city, as the final standard for the number of opium paste shops. Implement the Regulations for Suppressing Opium Paste Shops, purchase and sell opium paste with permits, and reduce sales year by year based on the quantity needed in the 24th year of the Republic, and also reduce the number of opium paste shops. Article 8: The Opium Suppression Supervisory Office is responsible for handling the suppression of transportation and sales. The civil affairs department of each province, the public security bureau of each city, the county magistrate, or the opium suppression committee shall be the responsible authorities for the suppression of opium cultivation and smoking and the suppression of smuggling within their respective jurisdictions. However, if the Opium Suppression Supervisory Office has specially established anti-smuggling agencies or patrol teams within its jurisdiction, the agency or team should be responsible for performing its duties in accordance with the anti-smuggling regulations. The local responsible authorities should assist at any time. Article 9: Each province, city, and county shall establish an opium suppression committee within one month. The committee shall be responsible for assisting in opium suppression and detoxification matters. (1) An opium suppression committee headquarters shall be established in the area where the Executive Headquarters is located, and fair and enthusiastic opium suppression advocates from all areas shall be appointed as members. (2) Opium suppression committees shall be established in each province and city. When necessary, the headquarters may send personnel to participate. (3) Opium suppression sub-committees shall be established in each county. Article 10: The expenses of the opium suppression committees and opium suppression sub-committees, detoxification centers, and opium addiction treatment centers established in each province, city, and county, as well as the subsidies for hospitals designated to handle detoxification and opium addiction treatment, shall be covered by the following items: (1) License fees for opium addicts and opium paste shops distributed by the British American Tobacco Company in the local area. (2) Opium suppression fines and the proceeds from the sale of confiscated drugs and the property of drug offenders. (3) Subsidies collected by the Opium Suppression Supervisory Office based on the fixed amount of opium sold in each province and city. (4) Special appropriations from various municipal treasuries. Article 11: The performance of local officials in handling opium suppression and anti-drug matters shall be specifically assessed. The senior officials of each province and city shall be responsible for assessing them once every three months, adding their comments, and reporting them to the Executive Headquarters for verification in a timely manner, in order to implement rewards and punishments based on the merits of opium suppression administration. The assessment regulations and reward and punishment measures will be determined separately. Article 12: The provinces of Sichuan, Yunnan, Guizhou, Chahar, Suiyuan, and Ningxia shall follow the precedent of phased opium suppression in Shaanxi and Gansu, and thoroughly investigate the number of counties, acreage, and output of opium production in each province within the 24th year of the Republic, as the standard for the final output, and draft a phased opium reduction plan and submit it to the Executive Headquarters for approval. Starting from the 25th year of the Republic, the reduction shall be phased in year by year. At the same time, the provinces of Hebei, Shandong, etc., should also be completely prohibited from opium cultivation, as in the inland provinces. Starting from the 25th year of the Republic, whether it is an absolutely prohibited or phased opium suppression province, the Executive Headquarters shall dispatch senior officials to implement inspections. Article 13: These measures shall be posted and announced by local military and government agencies within five days after receiving the official document of promulgation, so that all are aware. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Implementing Measures for Drug Suppression

(Hankou) Implementing Measures for Drug Suppression Article 1: Drug suppression procedures, in addition to following the Interim Regulations on Strictly Prohibiting Potent Drugs, shall be implemented in accordance with these measures. Article 2: If the number of people who use potent drugs or privately inject morphine in each province, city, and county is relatively large, drug rehabilitation centers should be established immediately. Starting from April of this year, provincial, municipal, and county governments are responsible for completing the establishment within three months, or expanding and merging with existing opium addiction treatment centers. However, in areas where the number of drug users is not large, drug rehabilitation may be administered in better hospitals as appropriate. Article 3: The provincial, municipal, and county governments should conduct on-site investigations at any time regarding the organization, equipment, rehabilitation procedures, and treatment methods of the drug rehabilitation centers or designated drug rehabilitation hospitals established in each province, city, and county, and whether they are appropriate, as well as the number of people undergoing rehabilitation and whether there are any increases or decreases, and report them to this Executive Headquarters for review on a monthly basis. The Executive Headquarters will select personnel with rich medical experience to go to various places to inspect, correct, and urge. Article 4: Anyone who manufactures, transports, or sells drugs shall be sentenced to death in accordance with regulations. Accomplices shall be sentenced to imprisonment of not less than five years but not more than twelve years, or life imprisonment, depending on the seriousness of the circumstances. However, public officials who assist in the manufacture, transportation, or sale of drugs shall be sentenced to death. Article 5: Houses used for drug production shall be confiscated. If they are rented, the landlord who knows but does not report shall be confiscated and handed over to the government, and the landlord shall be punished in the same way as an accomplice. From the 26th year of the Republic, anyone arrested for manufacturing, transporting, or selling drugs, whether the principal or an accomplice, shall be sentenced to death. Article 6: The private property of anyone who manufactures, transports, or sells drugs shall be investigated and confiscated. All informants and handlers shall be given a bonus of 20% to 40% of the confiscated property, depending on the circumstances. Article 7: Those who use potent drugs and inject morphine should automatically surrender to the center and quit completely within the 24th year of the Republic. If those who have not surrendered and are found to be using drugs privately are detained and sent to a drug rehabilitation center for counseling. In the 25th year of the Republic, if there are still those who have not surrendered and are using drugs privately, in addition to the detention and counseling mentioned above, they will also be sentenced to imprisonment of not less than five years. From the 26th year of the Republic, anyone who uses drugs and injects morphine shall be sentenced to death or life imprisonment. Article 8: Those who relapse after drug rehabilitation shall be sentenced to death in accordance with the regulations. However, those who voluntarily surrender for rehabilitation and relapse may be given a reduced sentence of imprisonment of not less than five years within the 24th year of the Republic. Article 9: Personnel from Party, government, military, and school institutions who use potent drugs or inject morphine are given a deadline to automatically surrender to the center for rehabilitation. Violators shall be sentenced to death. Article 10: These measures should be posted and announced by local military and government agencies within five days after receiving the official document of promulgation, along with the Interim Regulations on Strictly Prohibiting Potent Drugs promulgated by the Nanchang Executive Headquarters on May 11 of the 23rd year of the Republic, so that all are aware. They should also be summarized into simple explanations and explained and persuaded separately using the following methods: (1) In each city and county, the director of the public security bureau and the district head shall be responsible for organizing police officers and local officials in charge of autonomy and self-defense to regularly gather residents in their respective jurisdictions. (2) Party, government, military, and school institutions, as well as factories, should be organized regularly by the responsible personnel to gather their respective staff, soldiers, students, or workers. (3) Every three months, provinces and cities should jointly hold a large anti-drug propaganda meeting with Party, government, military, school, and other legal organizations, and may supplement it with recreational performances or costume parades to attract social attention. Article 11: Starting from the 24th year of the Republic, a general drug suppression inspection will be carried out once a year. The Executive Headquarters of the Military Affairs Commission will send personnel to conduct open and secret investigations in various places in order to assess the drug suppression achievements of each province, city, and county, and strictly implement rewards and punishments. Article 12: These measures will be implemented ten days after receiving the official document of promulgation. (Central News Agency dispatch on the 4th)

Chairman Chiang's Strict Order: Investigation and Prohibition of Opium Poppy Cultivation in Eight Provinces; Promulgation of General Reporting Methods, Swift and Effective Enforcement; Joint Responsibility by Special Envoys and Provincial Governments

Hankou dispatch: In order to thoroughly prohibit the cultivation of opium seedlings, Chairman Chiang has recently designated Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, and Henan provinces as absolute opium prohibition areas. General reporting methods have been formulated, and Wang Lie, Liu Weitan, and others have been appointed by the Executive Headquarters to jointly execute them with the respective provincial governments. The main points of the said methods, telegraphed to the military and political organs of each province on the 2nd for compliance, are recorded as follows: (1) Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Fujian, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hubei, and Henan provinces are designated as absolute opium prohibition provinces, while Shaanxi and Gansu provinces are designated as provinces with phased opium prohibition. All matters related to prohibiting sowing and investigating opium seedlings shall be the responsibility of the respective provinces. In order to promote investigation and prohibition and increase efficiency, special opium prohibition envoys dispatched by the Executive Headquarters of the Chairman of the Military Affairs Commission shall implement general reporting together with the provincial governments. (2) When implementing general reporting, in each administrative region, one or two committee members shall be dispatched by the provincial government's Civil Affairs Department, Security Department, administrative inspector, commissioner, and county government, to accompany the special envoy or jointly investigate and prohibit commissioners, and go to various counties, deep into rural areas, to carefully investigate and prohibit. The district chiefs and Baojia chiefs shall also accompany the inspection of all reporting matters. (3) The reporting period is limited to three months, from March to the end of May. If there are special circumstances, an extension may be requested, but the extension time shall not exceed one month. (4) All places where opium poppy cultivation has never existed and have been designated as absolute opium prohibition areas shall be subject to investigation. For counties where opium cultivation has never existed, after accurate verification, the administrative commissioner shall report to the provincial government and the special envoy for approval, and the county magistrate shall separately submit a written guarantee stating, "If opium seedlings are found to have emerged within the territory, I am willing to face the death penalty," and may be exempted from investigation, or subject to random checks as appropriate. (5) When opium seedlings are discovered during the implementation of general reporting, they shall be immediately uprooted, and the cultivating households shall be arrested and sent to legal authorities for prosecution, and the land shall be confiscated. If they defy the law and dare to gather crowds to resist, the stationed troops shall be allowed to strictly arrest the ringleaders, and a telegram shall be sent to the Executive Headquarters for approval, and they shall be executed immediately. (6) If opium seedlings are still found in counties that have been reported as opium-free after the investigation, the county magistrate, district chief, and Baojia chief of the county shall be jointly punished. The special envoy shall report the facts to the Executive Headquarters for strict punishment according to military law. (7) If it is found that unscrupulous military police units, officials, or local bullies dare to harbor opium cultivation or privately collect donations, the main persons shall be strictly arrested, and a telegram shall be sent to the Executive Headquarters for approval, and they shall be executed immediately. (8) When the special envoy implements general reporting together with the local government, if local military and political officials fail to implement effectively, thereby preventing them from exercising their powers and completing their tasks, the special envoy may report to the Executive Headquarters for instructions on how to handle it. (9) Each county for general reporting shall be divided into several districts, and held in phases. The location and date shall be determined by the special envoy or proposed by the investigation and prohibition commissioner and submitted to the special envoy for approval. (10) When general reporting is implemented, troops should be dispatched immediately to assist without delay. Commissioners or committee members at all levels may also bring police or troops to conduct on-site inspections in rural areas, but personnel and soldiers at all levels must be careful in handling matters and must not cause disturbances by taking advantage of the situation. (11) The investigation and prohibition commissioner shall report the reporting situation to the special envoy every day and forward it to the Executive Headquarters for review. (12) After inspecting each county, the special envoy shall list the actual reporting situation and the merits and demerits of the county's opium prohibition achievements in a detailed table and add a note, and forward it to the Executive Headquarters for assessment. The table format shall be separately determined. (13) The special envoy shall, together with the provincial government, strictly supervise its subordinates to earnestly proceed, and when necessary, still personally visit various districts for inspection. (14) The special envoy and the investigation and prohibition commissioner shall break away from personal feelings, seek truth from facts, and earnestly report. They shall not accept any entertainment from the local area or conceal information out of favor. Those who violate this shall be considered as colluding to act in self-interest. (15) If there are any omissions due to different circumstances in various provinces, the special envoy may, together with the provincial government, formulate implementing rules for supplementation. (16) These methods shall be implemented from the date of promulgation. (2nd)

Between Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao, Smuggling of Goods Increases Daily; More Than 500 People Involved in Smuggling; Qinhuangdao Customs Officers Wounded by Private Smugglers

Tianjin dispatch: Recently, incidents of Japanese smuggling of tax-evading goods between Shanhaiguan and Qinhuangdao have emerged endlessly. As a result, conflicts between customs and smugglers have also increased day by day. Last year, the Japanese used dozens of motorboats to transport goods such as ramie yarn, sugar, foreign cloth, and rayon from Dalian, Yingkou, and other places to the Shigekou and Duoluo River estuary for unloading. A group organized by the Japanese transported the goods to the Chadong area for distribution. Since the shooting of customs officers in Shigekou, although the dispute has been resolved, customs has paid special attention to the area, and tax police officers have been dispatched to patrol and permanently station there for permanent prevention. Japanese goods can no longer be imported as unimpeded as before. In early March of this year, with the prosperity of Huludao Port, Japanese cargo ships directly entered the port, and there was a railway connecting to Jinxi. The port was designated as the only tail waterway for smuggling. After the goods were landed, they were loaded onto vehicles and transported to Suizhong County, and then transported by camels from Suizhong to outside Shanhaiguan. They were then carried by small vendors over the Great Wall, avoiding the main roads of the checkpoints, and sent to Beidaihe or Qinhuangdao for delivery. The Japanese then used trucks to transport the goods to various counties and towns for dumping. Due to tax evasion, the price of every 100 yuan of goods can be reduced by 35%. Therefore, unscrupulous merchants in various cities are happy to accept illicit goods due to the great profit, and are willing to promote them, resulting in the flooding of Japanese goods in various places, which cannot be counted in numbers. This smuggling group is presided over by Japanese, and hires more than 500 Chinese traitors and Koreans to enter and exit Shanhaiguan inside and outside in shifts. Each person smuggles about 400 to 500 yuan of goods each time. Smuggling takes place at night, entering from the Jiao Mountain Temple next to Shanhaiguan, crossing the Great Wall. The private smugglers are armed with firearms, and resist with force when they encounter customs detectives. Therefore, customs personnel are wary. On the morning of the 28th of last month, Qinhuangdao detective Li Baohuan and a colleague patrolled to the side of the Beining Railway Bridge and encountered three smugglers transporting illicit goods. Just as they were about to step forward to search, the three smugglers suddenly took out guns and shot, causing Li to be hit by three bullets and fall to the ground. The three smugglers took the opportunity to escape. Li was rescued by his companion, his injuries were very serious, and he has been sent to Qinhuangdao Hospital for treatment. After this incident occurred, Hao Gede, the tax affairs director of Qinhuangdao, telegraphed the chief of the general customs of the Ministry of Finance to report and requested instructions on future investigation and patrol methods. On the 21st, near the South Great Temple of Shanhaiguan, customs personnel discovered nine large vehicles of Chinese traitors transporting illicit goods such as ramie yarn, intending to smuggle them across the Great Wall into the pass. The customs officers stopped them, and the accompanying Koreans opened fire. The customs officers returned fire in self-defense. The Korean and the Chinese traitor Wang Zihe fled to Dongluocheng. Before long, several Japanese military police officers from the customs arrived and arrested the customs officers, claiming that the goods were for military use and should not be seized. After customs personnel negotiated, the customs officers were released. Therefore, the customs officers felt that investigating and suppressing smuggling was becoming more and more difficult. (2nd)

The land and water police officers of the seven counties under the jurisdiction of the Second Police Inspection Area of this province have arrived in Songjiang. Yinyang: Design to Build a Gate in Huangtiangang

Huangtiangang is an important passage through the river, and is currently under construction for dredging. The Construction Department believes that the existing foot-skin gate is no longer applicable and must be rebuilt with a new type of ship lock. On the 2nd, it specially dispatched technician Guan Fuquan to Chengcheng to survey, intending to select a site between the port and Puhui Bridge. However, it requires a cost of 40,000 to 50,000 yuan. After the design is completed, the said cost will be borne by the Construction Department.

A Homicide Occurs Due to Two Boats Competing to Leave First

Zhang Xianglin, a boatman from Qian Nanzhang outside Wuxi, loaded wine in Xijing to Taixing the day before yesterday. Due to the breach of the dam in Huangtiangang, he changed his exit from Huangshangang. On the 2nd, when sailing through the Xiaoshang Bridge north of Zhouzhuang Sifting Pavilion, the Shanghai Tiebei boat following behind tried to pass first due to the crowding of boats, resulting in an argument. Zhang Rongkun and Zhang Zihe, the crew members of the Tiebei boat, fought with A Er, the crew member of the wine boat. A Er was hit in the waist with an iron bar and died on the spot. The case was reported to the Second District Office, which dispatched a merchant group to detain the assailants and reported to the county for an autopsy.

Wuxi: All County Opium Dens Reduce Fees

Recently, due to the county assembly’s approval of the forced opium addicts, the business of opium dens and smoking parlors in this county has been declining day by day. They have successively submitted requests to the county assembly to reduce the fees to maintain their operations. After receiving the submissions, the county assembly proposed them for discussion at the tenth regular meeting yesterday. It was resolved that the fees should be reduced by one level. Opium dens that previously paid the A level will pay the B level this term, and the B level will be changed to the C level. Smoking parlors that previously paid the A level will be changed to the B level, and the B level will be changed to the C level. Those who originally paid the C level will still pay the C level. In addition, the fourth batch of forced opium addicts should report to the county assembly for rehabilitation within the prescribed time limit.

Grand Occasion of Various Circles Celebrating Children's Day

Yesterday was Children's Day on April 4th. Various circles in this county enthusiastically celebrated and blessed the children. At 9:00 am, it was held in the Wuxi Grand Theater in the park. County Magistrate Yan Shenyu, representatives of party and government agencies, students from various schools, and people from all walks of life enthusiastically participated. Xu Chizi was appointed as chairman. After performing the ceremony, Xu Chizi (Party Committee), Hu (Director of the Education Bureau), and other members of the presidium gave speeches in succession. Then, guests from all walks of life, Liu Xueying (female) from Yudaiqiao Primary School, and Mr. Huang Jiping from Shanghai Kunbao Newspaper gave speeches. Finally, children Xia Shiguo (Central), Yu Hao (Yang), and Zhang Zuji (Tang) gave speeches. Subsequently, photos were taken, and Mr. Huang from Shen Bao presented the "Children's Friend" and "Children's Day Commemorative Album" published by the newspaper. The meeting adjourned at 11:00 am. At 3:00 pm, the County Education Association held a celebration meeting for model children. Li Tiping chaired the meeting. After the meeting, all the model children went to the county government to meet County Magistrate and Bureau Director. County Magistrate Yan and Bureau Director Zang gave speeches, and the children's representatives gave thanks before dispersing.

Changshu: Resolution of the Rice Industry Strike

The rice industry strike has lasted for three days. Yesterday (the 3rd) at 3:00 pm, the party and government authorities, based on yesterday's resolution, summoned the rice merchants in charge to the county for talks. County Magistrate Qu Huan, Party Secretary An Weinan, Chairman Pang Jiegong of the Chamber of Commerce, and representatives of the Public Security Bureau attended. On the rice industry side, there were Chairman Wen Yaowen of the Guild and Executive Committee member Lu Gongquan and more than ten others. County Magistrate Qu earnestly persuaded them, but at first the rice industry refused to mediate and demanded that Director Liu be dismissed before they would resume business. As a result, the losses were too great, and the director was not under the jurisdiction of the county government. After about two hours of discussion, the rice industry representatives agreed to resume business on the 4th. As for the tax reduction issue, it will be negotiated later. Therefore, this storm can be said to have come to an end.

Kunshan: Director of Civil Affairs Visits Kunshan for Inspection

Yu Jingtang, Director of Civil Affairs of Jiangsu Province, arrived in Kunshan from Suzhou at 9:00 am on the 4th. After the car arrived at the county government, he summoned officials from various agencies to give a speech in the auditorium. Then, he inspected the county government, the Public Security Bureau, the Education Bureau, the County Party Headquarters, and the County Opium Prohibition Office. At noon, County Magistrate Peng hosted a banquet at the government to entertain Director Yu and others, and invited Wei Wenyuan, the chairman of the County Chamber of Commerce, and others to accompany them. At 1:30 pm, he took the Beijing-Zha Joint Transportation train and transferred to Yunshan.

Haimen: Party Committee Sued Case Declared Not Guilty

Former County Party Committee Executive Committee members Chen Bingzi, Cao Dingshi, Huang Chenggong, and Supervisory Committee member Mao Dingyi were accused by Shi Shulan, Fan Qinliang, and others last April of deteriorating and betraying the party, protecting bandits and accepting bribes, and other charges were submitted to the Central Party Headquarters. The Central Organization Committee sent Wan Jun to Haimen to investigate. Regarding the alleged charges, it was deemed that there were indeed suspicions, so Chen and others were suspended and transferred to the Shanghai Local Court for detention and investigation. Now Chen and others have presented evidence of rebuttal. After repeated trials by the court, the truth was revealed, and they were declared innocent and released the day before yesterday. Yesterday, Chen and the other four returned to Hai from Shanghai.

Robber Den Broken Up Near the Temple of the Sea God

Tianbuzhen in the Second District is located in the eastern township of Kunlian Nantong, which has always been an area where bandits haunt. Now that the time of year when the old harvest is exhausted and the new has not yet come, generally unscrupulous elements are taking the opportunity to stir up trouble, so more than ten robbery cases have occurred there in the past month, which is shocking to hear. Yesterday (the 2nd), Zhu Ziye, the patrol officer of the Public Security Sub-station of the town, learned that there was a robber den near the Temple of the Sea God, so he led all the police officers to search. He arrested Xu Shicai, Xu Shilai, Wu Yongxiang, 　Xianlin, Huang A’gen, and Ge Xu and other 14 people, and confiscated many stolen certificates. There are still wanted criminals Ge Zhengxing, Zhang Jinqing, etc., who resisted arrest by firing guns, and were escaped. That night, after Zhu patrol officer questioned them, the bandits confessed without denial. They were all escorted to the county government for trial today (the 3rd).

Danyang: The Old Irrigation Mouth of Xiangcao River Is Breached

Zhong Xilin, director of the Xiangcao River Dredging Project Office, said that the land near the old irrigation mouth tributary dam was low-lying and connected to Lianhu Lake. Recently, due to continuous strong winds and heavy rains, mountain water poured into Lianhu Lake and directly impacted the tributary of the dam. At about 7 pm on March 27, the supervisor reported that the water level in the dam had risen about two inches above the top of the dam, and the water was surging. Zhong director learned of this and urgently sent more than 60 workers to the dam along the coast to dig soil and check the danger, which lasted all night. However, the water was surging and breaches were occurring everywhere, resulting in the inundation of the entire section, reaching a depth of about two meters. He immediately reported the situation to Bi County Magistrate, who was also the director of the Xiangcao River project. After receiving the report, County Magistrate Bi immediately went to inspect it for a week, took photos, and ordered the Zhen workers in Jintan County to temporarily return to Lair to wait for the water to be drained before being notified to start work. The matter has been reported to the Construction Department, requesting that personnel be dispatched to conduct an on-site inspection.

Nantong: Mangxia Village Town Robbed by Bandits

Mangxia Village Town in the east of the city was robbed by bandits at about 2 am on the 3rd. Dinglong Yarn Shop, Yonglong Dyeing Shop, and Yulong Noodle Shop suffered heavy losses. The bandits searched and looted for two hours before firing guns and escaping with the stolen goods. The district office reported to the county government for inspection and sent a security team to pursue the escaped bandits, but they were not captured.

Holding an Opium Prohibition Speech Contest

The Nantong Opium Prohibition Committee and the Education Bureau have scheduled to hold a speech contest for primary school students on opium prohibition on the 14th of this month. The county will be divided into six school districts, and the contest will be held simultaneously. Each school will send three contestants to participate.

Yangzhou: Director Orders Agricultural Bank to Release Seedling Loans

In the disaster areas of Jiangdu 8 and 9, the loan for work and disaster relief and seeds requires a lot of funds. Methods for raising funds have been repeatedly reported in this newspaper. The Finance Department plans to provide disaster relief funds to the two disaster areas, but it is not easy to raise funds. It has ordered the Provincial Farmers Bank to launch seedling loans and instructed Jiangdu County Magistrate Ma Zhenbang to send personnel to contact the bank to discuss and implement the matter.

Jiashan: Results of Bribery Case Trial

In the Cheng surname mansion in Fengjing Town, Su Daiyu, Cheng Xingbai, and others set up a gambling den and entrusted Cheng Peiren, the town mayor, to bribe Qiu Zeshen, the director of the Public Security Sub-bureau, with 20 yuan of foreign currency every day. The case was secretly reported to the provincial government by gentlemen and merchants in the town. The provincial government sent Yang Jinbiao, a police instructor from Shan-Jia, to investigate and verify the facts, which caused a sensation in Shanghai. The society has been paying attention to it. It is learned that the county court specially opened an investigation court yesterday. Prosecutor Zhang Bingsheng interrogated in court in great detail. As a result, Cheng Peiren (the town mayor who offered the bribe) was released on bail for 300 yuan. Qiu Zeshen was detained because he did not have 500 yuan in cash. The court is still offering rewards for the arrest of the main culprits.

Hangzhou: The Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Boy Scout Congress

The Fourth Zhejiang Provincial Boy Scout Congress was held yesterday (4th) at 9:00 am at the Naxing Bridge camp in Hangzhou. 3,450 scouts were reviewed, and they successively assembled from the Wansongling camp to the main camp in detachments. Twenty-one cannons were fired to open the congress, followed by the flag raising. Xu Shaodi, Director of Education, presided over the ceremony. After the ceremony, the review was conducted. The reviewers were Huang Shaoji, Wang Tingyang, Ji Zhirou, Yi Tiewu, Zheng Wenli, and others. At 10:00, all the scouts gathered in front of the podium. Xu Shaodi gave a speech, encouraging the scouts to realize their responsibilities, strengthen their physique, and be the backbone of the nation. Then, Feng Ti, a representative of the China Boy Scouts General Association, gave a speech, followed by Huang Shaohong, Fang Qingru, and others. The meeting adjourned at 11:30. Starting at 1:00 pm, curriculum performances were held. A lantern parade was held in the evening.

Huzhou: Fire in Zhicheng Road

There is a Sun surname house in a small alley opposite the Dongwu Hotel on Zhicheng Road in this city. It was rented to the Zhida Cigarette Company as a warehouse. The remaining houses were sublet by Zhida to Zheng Jingfu, the owner of the Dasheng Paper Store, and his brother Shunfu, etc., and the warehouse of the paper store was also inside. Unexpectedly, at about 4:00 am this morning (the 3rd), a fire suddenly broke out in the house. The neighbors were awakened from their dreams and went to try to rescue. However, it took an hour of burning before it was extinguished. As a result, all six or seven houses and the goods stored in the warehouses of the two families, as well as the clothes and ornaments in the inner rooms of Zheng Jingfu and his brothers, were all burned to ashes.

Ningbo: Bandit Resists Arrest and Shoots Police Officer

Li Xiangqi, captain of the Fenghua County Daqiao Garrison, received a tip that a bandit named Qiu Yongfa, wearing a military uniform, was hiding in the house of a certain Jia near the North Gate Public Stadium. He reported to the general regiment and the county Public Security Bureau to dispatch eight or nine police officers, led by Li Xiangqi, to the address for arrest at about 10:00 pm the night before yesterday (the 1st). Unexpectedly, as soon as the captain entered, the bandit drew a wooden-cased gun and shot him. Captain Li was shot in the waist and seriously injured. At the same time, a police officer named Chen Guang was shot in the head and died instantly. The bandit then fled to Xikou. Fortunately, the Third Public Security Sub-bureau had sent three police officers, Ma Wenchang and others, to guard the pass. They encountered Qiu Bandit. The bandit raised his gun to shoot and shot and killed police officer Ma Wenchang. At that time, the other two police officers also returned fire, but due to the late hour, he still escaped. Afterwards, the police officer returned to the bureau and reported everything.

Xiaoshan: Establishment of the Eastern Township Sericulture Guidance Center

The eastern township of Xiaoshan is an area that produces silk cocoons. Silk farming households are lined up and mulberry trees are everywhere. Because all silk farming households are not improved, sales have decreased greatly in recent years. Since the establishment of the Sericulture Guidance Center by the Provincial Construction Department last year to promote improved seeds, the sales of silk cocoons have gradually developed. This year, the Sericulture Guidance Center was officially established on April 1. At that time, in addition to dispatching personnel from the Fifth and Sixth Districts to guide, Ms. Zuo Suzhen was dispatched by the province to Xiaoshan to guide households. On the one hand, three major cases were resolved: (1) After each silk farming household releases silkworms, women instructors will guide them separately. (2) Banning the mixing of other species or native species. (3) After the improved species are raised by silk farming households, the price of new cocoons will be increased.

International Commercial Telecommunications – Special Reuters Commercial Report of April 4th –

Gold and Silver

London gold prices fell due to the high price of the pound sterling. Today's listing is 144 shillings and 3 pence, down 1 shilling and 4.5 pence from yesterday.

The London silver market saw little trading, and prices fell slightly. The spot price is 25 pence 3125, and futures are 28 pence 375, both down 0625 from yesterday. India and China are both buying and selling, and the market is stable.

Exchange Rates

The Anglo-American London exchange market opened stable this morning, with demand for the pound sterling. The opening price for Anglo-American exchange was $4.82875, up one-eighth of a pound from yesterday's US-British close. At 11:00 AM, it continued to rise by half an eighth of a pound. Later, due to reduced demand, prices reversed. At 1:00 PM, the price was $4.82625, down seven-eighths, but at 2:00 PM, the price rose again to $4.83125, because there were more buyers.

The Anglo-French exchange fluctuated narrowly. The opening price was 73 francs 15, up 28 eighths of a pound from yesterday's close. At 11:00 AM, it rose 11 eighths of a pound to 73 francs 25. After that, it gradually declined for two hours. At 1:00 PM, the price was 73 francs 12. Later, the market stabilized, and at 2:00 PM, the price was 73 francs 21, up 6 eighths of a pound from the opening. The decision to mint gold coins in France does not appear to have had much impact on the market.

The US-British New York foreign exchange market saw a slightly higher opening for the pound sterling, with the price at $4.83125, up one and one-quarter cents from yesterday's close, due to high demand for the pound. However, it later fell back slightly. The US-French exchange opened at $6.60125, down seven-eighths of a cent from yesterday.

Cotton and Wheat

New York cotton market rose slightly at the opening today due to higher Liverpool telegrams. Agricultural Secretary Wallace's statement that there may not be any changes to the cotton handling donation before August 1st was not well received by the cotton market, and protests are expected. The report of insect pests in Brazilian cotton production has not yet been detailed, and everyone is awaiting further reports.

Chicago wheat remained firm today due to better overseas telegrams, and disappointing rainfall in the early areas. The wheat market is fundamentally solid, and international market sentiment has recently greatly improved.

Liverpool wheat: The overseas market is better, and the weather report is still unfavorable, so the Liverpool wheat market is in good spirits. At 1:00 PM, the July contract price was 5 shillings 7 pence 75, up 1 penny from yesterday's close.

Liverpool cotton: Today the market situation is quite pleasant due to better buying. At 1:00 PM, the July contract price was 6.08, up 4 eighths of a pound from yesterday's close.

Rubber

London opened stable today, with prices fluctuating within a very small range. The trading price for the July contract at noon was 5 pence 8125, the same as yesterday's price.

New York's market situation was better today, and prices rose slightly, because the closing sentiment yesterday turned firm, and the London telegram was stable again. The statistical position is showing signs of improvement.

Securities

New York opened today without any excitement. Only a few stocks rose slightly in price due to speculative buying. Most of the others remained unchanged, with some prices falling slightly. The New York securities market prices are listed on the left:
