Local News

Yesterday was the 5th Annual Children's Day The City Celebrated Enthusiastically More Than 5,000 Children Participated in the Celebration Ceremony The Children's Film Day was Unveiled by Director Pan Various Groups and Schools Participated in the Celebration Separately

Shanghai News Agency reports that yesterday was the 5th Annual Children's Day in China. The city's Party and government organs held a celebration ceremony at the Moonlight Grand Theatre at 9:00 AM. Approximately 5,000 children participated. At the same time, the Children's Film Day opened. The mayor was temporarily unable to attend due to matters and Director Pan represented the opening ceremony. Various groups and schools also held celebrations separately. Stores throughout the city reduced prices and parks were opened to treat children favorably. The situation was quite enthusiastic. The details are recorded as follows:

Joint Celebration by Party and Government Organs

A Glimpse of the Venue

The Children's Day celebration jointly held by the city's Party Department and the Children's Welfare Association, along with various agencies and organizations, took place at the Moonlight Grand Theatre on Baille Road. The Party and national flags were hung high at the entrance of the theater, and a white cloth banner with the artistic characters "Shanghai City All Sectors Celebrating Children's Day Commemorative Fire Meeting" was hung. Inside the entrance of the venue, a banner with "Children's Film Day Unveiling Ceremony" was hung. Bright slogans were posted throughout the venue, and the celebration environment was decorated. The Health Bureau specially set up a temporary medical station in the folds to take charge of rescue matters. The Boy Scout Council specially sent the Council to maintain order at the venue. Photographed by Xu Tianzhang.

Participating Representatives

Including Director Pan of the City Education Bureau, Jiang Huaisu of the City Party Department, Li Dachao of the Municipal Government, Li Ting'an of the Health Bureau, Cai Jingjun of the Public Security Bureau, Hu Shuyi of the Children's Welfare Association, Chen Lengseng representing the Social Affairs Bureau, Chen Tiesheng of the Child Welfare Association, Wang Jiyi of the City Security Department, and representatives from various elementary schools such as Wanzhu, Xicheng, He'an, Feihong, Shangwen, Danhua, and Linyin, totaling more than 5,000 people. Both upstairs and downstairs were fully seated. Qian Fugong, the general director of the organizing committee, Lin Kecong, a member of the organizing committee, staff members Yuan Zengyu and Zhou Wanghe, Xu Gongmei of the Children's Film Committee, and Hu Xuguang of the Moonlight Grand Theatre personally took on the reception duties. The orchestra of orphans played music.

Holding Ceremony

At 9:00 AM, the celebration ceremony was held. The presidium included Pan Gongzhan, Li Ting'an, Cai Jingjun, Hu Shuyi, Wu Xingya (represented by Chen Lengseng), Yang Xiaotian (represented by Wang Jiyi), Chen Jicheng, Lin Kecong, and Chen Tiesheng. The master of ceremonies was He Yuanming, and the recorders were Du Mengsen and Tong Muge. First, Director Pan represented Mayor Wu in unveiling the Children's Film Day and delivered an opening speech. Then, Li Ting'an of the City Health Bureau and Jiang Huaisu of the City Party Department delivered speeches. Lin Kecong delivered a speech, followed by a response from Gu Senbao, a student from Danhua Elementary School, representing the children. Then, slogans were shouted and performances were held before the event was dismissed.

Chairman's Report

Chairman Director Pan reported, stating briefly, "Today is the anniversary of the Children's Day of the 24th year of the Republic of China. Originally, Mayor Wu was supposed to come in person to deliver a speech, but due to other important matters, I am representing him. The Chinese Child Welfare Association and the Children's Welfare Association have presented to the National Government and stipulated April 4th as Children's Day. This is now the fifth year. Recently, it has been presented to the National Government and stipulated that August 1st of this year will be Children's Year. Today, Party, government, and various organizations are jointly holding a grand celebration, which shows that the government and society attach great importance to children. Everyone knows that China is now very dangerous, but does not know that the future world situation is even more serious. China's danger will be even greater in the future than it is today. Rescuing the danger now relies on adults, and in the future, it will rely on you children. While you are still minors, the government will of course find ways to educate you and nurture you, so that your bodies, knowledge, morals, and abilities all have a foundation, so that you can save the country from danger in the future. Therefore, the first significance of celebrating Children's Day today is that you will contribute to the country and the nation in the future. Second, there are three to four hundred thousand school-age children in Shanghai, and only a few thousand people are here today. There are still many children who do not have the opportunity to participate, and even do not have enough to eat and struggle on the line of life and death. You are fortunate to participate in this, and you must help other children anytime, anywhere. Through this celebration meeting, we also call on the majority of adults in society to pay attention to the education of general children. Third, Shanghai is the focus of national attention, and every move is enough to affect the whole country. The order and discipline of the children participating in the Shanghai celebration meeting is related to the children of the whole country. Therefore, you children of Shanghai have a greater responsibility than other places. You should be a model for children across the country."

Party and Government Speeches

Director Li Ting'an of the Health Bureau said, in brief, "The meaning of holding a children's celebration today is to seek the interests of children. Children are the future masters of China. You must create yourselves and hope that the mothers of Shanghai will pay special attention to the education of children," and so on. Jiang Huaisu, a member of the City Party Department, said, in brief, "On this day commemorating Children's Day, I hope for two points: (1) I hope that educational authorities and social figures will find ways to solve the problem of children not attending school. (2) I hope that all parents will pay attention to children's health issues." Lin Kecong also had a speech, which is omitted.

Children's Response

Gu Senbao, a student from Danhua Elementary School representing the children, said in brief, "Ladies and gentlemen, children, today, all sectors of Shanghai are holding a Children's Day celebration ceremony here. Just now, many teachers have guided us, and everyone has understood it. Now, I respectfully represent the children of Shanghai to thank all the teachers, and I hope that all the children will follow what the teachers have guided us to do and not disappoint the teachers' enthusiasm," and so on.

Assembly Slogans

(1) Children are the future masters of the new China. (2) Children are the cornerstone of building a new China. (3) Children are the inheritors of the Chinese nation. (4) Children are the new force for the revival of the Chinese nation. (5) Intensify the education and training of children. (6) Children must bear the responsibility of the Three Principles of the People. (7) Let's all celebrate Children's Day. (8) Long live the Chinese nation. (9) Long live the Three Principles of the People. (10) Long live the Chinese Nationalist Party.

Entertainment and Gifts

After the celebration ceremony, Wanzhu, He'an, Danhua, Xicheng, Shangwen, Feihong, Wuben, Qimei, Bide, Yangzheng, and Linyin schools performed entertainment, and the meeting distributed a bag of gifts to each child. From 1:30 PM onwards, children's films were screened at the Moonlight Grand Theatre, and China-Europe Sugar Factory and Wuzhou Pharmacy sent gum and herbal soap to each person on the spot.

Celebration Ceremony of the Child Welfare Association

Celebration Assembly

The Chinese Child Welfare Association, together with the Zhabei Child Welfare Sanatorium, Child Welfare Clinic, Child Welfare Daycare Center, and Civilian Education Institute, held a celebration assembly at the Civilian Education Institute yesterday morning at 10:00 AM. More than 300 orphans participated. The chairman was Yao Shuren. After performing the ceremony, the chairman gave a report, followed by a speech by Wu Weide, and a speech by the representative of the Education Bureau. Then, students from the Civilian Education Institute performed entertainment before the event was dismissed.

Health Competition

The children's health competition organized by the association has ended. A total of 72 children participated in the infant group, 69 in the kindergarten group, and 458 in the young children group. After the judges' evaluation, 5 children in the infant group were awarded super-class, 5 special-class, 1 in the kindergarten group was awarded super-class, 6 special-class, 3 excellent-class, 1 in the young children group A was awarded super-class, 2 special-class, 4 excellent-class, 1 in the young children group B was awarded super-class, 3 special-class, 4 excellent-class, and 2 in the young children group C were awarded super-class, 2 special-class, 6 excellent-class.

Awarding Prizes

At 2:00 PM yesterday afternoon, an award ceremony was held in the auditorium of the Civilian Education Institute. After Chairman Li Ting'an performed the ceremony, the chairman delivered an opening speech, followed by Liu Yide reporting on the inspection situation. Then, Mrs. Li Ting'an awarded prizes before a photograph was taken and the event was dismissed.

Educational Groups Celebrate Separately

Civic Education Center

The Municipal Public Education Center on Wenshu Road in the southern city of Nanshi held a toy exhibition yesterday to commemorate Children's Day. Dozens of toys were collected, including construction blocks from the Xin'yi Toy Company and military models from the New Era Educational Supplies Company, which were quite wonderful. The center also held an entertainment assembly from 7:00 PM onwards, with programs including singing, dancing, dramas, and magic. The Children's Day Celebration Preparatory Committee also collected gifts and distributed them on the spot. Opening of the Children's Day Commemorative Assembly (Photographed by Qi Yueyue)

Various Elementary Schools

Yesterday, which coincided with the spring break period, each elementary school, in addition to sending four representatives to participate in the joint celebration ceremony, also held a simple celebration ceremony at the school, inviting children from outside the school to participate. The principals of each school reported on the meaning of Children's Memorial Day, and there were also entertainment performances and achievement exhibitions, etc.

Mandarin Church

The National Mandarin Education Promotion Association held a 4-4 celebration meeting at the Shanghai Radio Station in Jinxing Building yesterday afternoon at 4:00 PM. Lu Yiyan delivered an opening speech, and children broadcasted programs totaling 44 sections, including singing, speeches, storytelling, music, and dramas.

Children's Education Groups

Other organizations, such as the Chinese Children's Culture Association, invited Tao Zhixing and Wei Bingxin to give speeches at the China-West Radio Station at 10:00 AM yesterday morning. The Shanhai Children's Society held an inauguration ceremony at Dacha yesterday morning, inviting Jiang Kanghu to give a speech and perform entertainment. Huacun Public Basic School held a children's song and dance party and a children's tea party in Xinjing. The Children's Life Education Group held an inauguration ceremony at Yu Tang at 9:00 AM yesterday morning, with a speech by Niu Yongjian. The rural improvement area in the suburbs of Shanghai held a celebration assembly at the Public Sports Field.

Society Also Celebrates

Parks Open

All parks in the city, such as the French Park, Zhaofeng Park, Hongkou Park, and the Bund Park, were open all day yesterday to invite children to visit the park. Hospitals provided free physical examinations and vaccinations for children. Stores reduced prices to treat children favorably.

Broadcasts and Lectures

The Shipping Radio Station broadcasted children's programs exclusively from 9:00 AM yesterday morning to 6:00 PM, with speeches by Mayor Wu, Director Pan, Director Cai, Yu Qiaqing, Wang Xiaolai, Chen Heqin, Hu Shuyi, Wang Xiaoying, and Liu Wangliming. Wuben, Wanzhu, Danhua, and other schools participated in singing.

Broadcasting Competition

The Shanghai Children's Broadcasting Competition jointly organized by the Shanghai Guangpan Radio Station and the China National Goods Company was held yesterday as the first day of the competition. It was the Group A competition, from 2:30 PM to 5:00 PM. The program included 9 sections of music, 2 sections of speeches, and 21 sections of singing.

Two Newspapers Celebrate

This newspaper regards children as the future masters of the Republic of China, so it printed 200,000 copies of the Children's Day commemorative book and sent it along with the newspaper yesterday. The book included a half-price discount coupon for "Children's Friend." The content of the book is divided into twelve chapters: (1) Children's Forum, (2) Children's Science, (3) Handicrafts, (4) Common Knowledge, (5) Anecdotes of Celebrities, (6) Civic Training, (7) Poems, (8) Pictures, (9) Children's Literature, (10) Children's Health, (11) Stories, (12) Entertainment, totaling more than 200,000 words, with beautiful paintings and lively illustrations, making it suitable for everyone to have a copy. The News and the News Evening News held a reader's children's garden party in Bansongyuan, South City, yesterday. 10,000 admission tickets were issued in advance. A large auditorium was specially set up in the park. The celebration ceremony began at 2:00 PM in the afternoon. Chairman Wang Boqi delivered a speech, Yan Duhe reported, and Sun Yucai, a representative of the Education Bureau, and educator Chen Jicheng gave speeches. Then, students from various schools and kindergartens participated in singing performances, as well as other songs, dances, and harmonica programs.

President Wang is Coming to Shanghai To Host a Banquet for Chinese and Foreign Dignitaries Time… 7:30 PM on the 7th Address… Shanghai Municipal Government Auditorium

Central News Agency reports that Executive Yuan President Wang plans to attend the International Exhibition of Chinese Art in London and hold a preview exhibition in Shanghai. He will hold a banquet for Chinese and foreign dignitaries at 7:30 PM on the 7th of this month (Sunday) at the Shanghai Municipal Government Auditorium. It is reported that those invited include the presidents and ministers of various central departments, military attachés from various countries, and more than 100 leaders from various agencies and sectors in the city. At that time, there will be a constant stream of cars and horses, which will be extremely grand.

Three Banks to Rescue Industry and Commerce Negotiating Methods in the Shortest Term

Central News Agency reports that in order to strengthen the capital of the Central, China, and Communications Banks and to rescue the decline of industry and commerce, the Ministry of Finance has issued 100 million yuan in financial public bonds. According to the Central News Agency reporter's inquiry with the financial community, the financial public bonds are entirely for rescuing the market and have been properly allocated, but they are not circulating on the market, only used as a reserve for issuing banknotes. In this way, in the midst of the current market downturn, a batch of active cash can be indirectly increased for industry and commerce to mortgage and borrow, and the market can circulate.

Negotiating Methods in the Nearest Term

The three banks are based on this purpose and are working together, so in the short term, they will organize a banking group to facilitate progress. According to the Central News Agency reporter's inquiry with the banking sector, the Central, China, and Communications Banks will negotiate methods in the short term to quickly rescue the decline of industry and commerce and facilitate progress. The time will be approximately after the implementation of the 5 million yuan industrial and commercial credit small loan.

Underwriting Mortgages and Circulating the Market

It is heard that the three banks' rescue methods will still focus on mortgage loans. Currently, the market is declining, and the banking sector is timid and does not dare to underwrite large mortgage loans because there is no large amount of capital and they are afraid of facing turnover difficulties. Now, with increased capital and cooperation, all industries can obtain financial assistance, and the circulation will be smooth and lively, then the market will improve, which is naturally expected.

Kong Xiangxi and Others Arrive in Shanghai

Kong Xianxi and Ju Zheng took the overnight express train from Beijing yesterday and arrived in Shanghai this morning.

Song Ziwen Regularly Meets with Journalists Foreign Telegraphs Spread Unconfirmed Stories of Monetary Conference

New News Agency reports that since taking over as Chairman of the Board of Directors of the Bank of China, Song Ziwen, a standing committee member of the National Economic Council, has been going to the bank for days to handle various important official duties and has been extremely busy. Because the outside world is quite concerned about the future business policy of the Bank of China, Song has specially set aside the 9th (next Tuesday) to openly meet with reporters from various newspapers on the third floor of the Bank of China on Hankou Road Bund to make remarks and elaborate on the future facilities of the Bank of China and opinions on rescuing finance. Regarding the propaganda by Havas Agency on the 2nd that the government will follow the British suggestion and invite representatives from the banking sectors of Britain, France, the United States, Japan, and Belgium to hold a monetary conference in Beijing, Zhu believes that this is inaccurate. He believes that even if China needs to discuss the issue of unifying the monetary system in fact, there is no need to invite foreign bankers to participate.

Zhang Fakui Visited Mayor Wu Yesterday Morning Does Not Intend to Linger in Shanghai Plans to Fly to Sichuan and Transfer to Guizhou to Meet Chiang in the Coming Days

Central Committee Member Zhang Fakui, after wandering overseas and returning to China, entered Beijing from Shanghai last month to visit various central authorities and friends in Beijing, and to discuss matters. After the entertainment in Beijing was completed, he left Beijing by car on the morning of the 3rd, returned to Shanghai along the Beijing-Hangzhou National Road. 法租界 Taxpaying Chinese Association Protests Increased Levies and Power Outages; Requests Immediate Restoration of Water and Electricity and Negotiation of Tax Amounts by Industry

The French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association, based on a complaint from the Fourth District Branch of the Second Special District Citizens' Federation regarding member Ju Shun Yi Sauce Garden on 187 Ximen Road, which was subjected to increased alcohol tax and electricity cut-off by the French Municipal Council, sent a letter of protest to the French Municipal Council yesterday. The original letter is transcribed below:

Respectfully,

According to a letter from the Fourth District Branch of the Second Special District Citizens' Federation, Ju Shun Yi Sauce Garden at 187 Ximen Road reports that in September of last year, the French Municipal Council increased the original alcohol tax from $2.80 to $7.00. We then wrote to your association to request the French Concession Taxpaying Chinese Association to negotiate with the French Municipal Council. Subsequently, the director of the Bureau personally investigated, and in December, the tax collector collected the accumulated tax arrears for four months (totaling $11.20) and indicated that the increased tax might be cancelled in the future. On February 28th of this year, we suddenly received a letter from the Bureau stating that our alcohol tax was set at $5.00 per month, with two months in arrears, requiring a supplementary payment of $10.00 within three days, or else water and electricity would be cut off. After translating and reading this, we were extremely perplexed. Our business of Shaoxing wine is very small in scale, unlike specialized Shaoxing wine businesses, and we have records to prove this. Now, the French Municipal Council's collection of a third-class monthly tax is already excessive. If it is suddenly increased to $5.00, it will be even more unfair. While we were requesting assistance from your association, the electricity was actually cut off on March 25th. We specifically request your association to uphold justice and provide swift relief.

Upon investigation, the case of the increased tax for this business was previously negotiated by your association. Now, the electricity has been cut off, oppressing merchants, which is improper in both law and reason. Therefore, we request your association to urge the French Municipal Council to improve the temporary rules for cutting off water and electricity, in order to secure business. Cutting off water and electricity is contrary to the intention of the municipal authorities to care for merchants and residents. The improvement measures requested by the association are deeply reasonable. In addition to separate letters to the Chinese directors, we jointly request your honorable Municipal Council to first restore the electricity to the business, collect the accumulated original tax according to the original amount, and in the future, for similar incidents, the sauce and wine industries in the French Concession should determine the tax amounts separately according to their respective levels, in order to avoid disputes. Whether or not to adopt this measure, we pray for your wise decision and prompt reply, so that we may inform them accordingly.

Yangtze River Steamers Increase Schedules; Yueyang Maru Resumes Service

The Nisshin Kisen Kaisha Yangtze River steamers originally had eleven vessels. In the upper and middle reaches of the Yangtze River, there were another fourteen vessels, with business equal to that of Butterfield & Swire and Jardine Matheson, and larger than that of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company. After the January 28th Incident, due to boycotts in various ports, the company's Yangtze River ships were all suspended. After three years of planning, only four ships, such as the Luoyang Maru and Nanyang Maru, were restored to service. Only one ship was opened on the upper reaches of the Yangtze. Recently, the import of Japanese goods into China has greatly increased, with Nisshin Kisen Kaisha cargo ships arriving at the docks fully loaded each time. The cargo transferred to the Yangtze River has increased by another one-half compared to before. The Nisshin Kisen Kaisha has taken advantage of this great opportunity to restore the Yangtze River ships that had been suspended for more than three years to their normal schedules. The Yueyang Maru has been repaired and completed and has summoned all of the disbanded crew and sailors, and from April 2nd, has joined the Shanghai-Hankou line. Currently, the company has five ships operating on the Yangtze River route. The company is also planning to restore the remaining suspended ships step by step.

Ministry of Railways Telegraph Reply to the Banking Association Regarding Railway Bills of Lading

The Ministry of Railways telegraphed a reply to the Shanghai Banking Association, stating that the improvement of railway bills of lading is under discussion by the Ministry. Currently, the Association is requested to inform all member banks and advise merchants to exchange for bills of lading. In the future, receipts for goods stored in yards and freight receipts will not be accepted for mortgages. Furthermore, if station staff members deliberately delay or refuse to issue bills of lading when merchants apply for them, please report this immediately to the Ministry or the local railway bureaus. Once verified, they will be punished. In addition to ordering each railway to actively promote bills of lading, and sending personnel to inspect and supervise the handling of each station, a deadline has been set for reporting the situation. This telegram is for your information.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce Telegraphs Ministry of Finance, Requesting Prompt Abolition of National Goods Transit Tax and Appropriate Increase of Import Tax to Offset the Loss

The Shanghai Chamber of Commerce telegraphed the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing, stating:

Respectfully to the Ministry of Finance in Nanjing,

On the 3rd of this month, a joint letter from the Chinese Paper Mill Federation, the China National Goods Maintenance Association, and the Shanghai Citizens Promoting National Goods Association stated that the domestically produced products of Chinese mechanized factories, when transported to various provinces for sale, are required to pay transit taxes. Your association and national factory organizations have repeatedly requested the government to exempt these taxes, but no action has been taken. Currently, our national products are suffering from the dumping of foreign goods, coupled with the impact of low gold prices and high silver prices. The national industries are in imminent danger and are barely surviving. We previously read in the newspapers that Minister Kong spoke about immediately removing import taxes, which was submitted to the Executive Yuan for approval, and would be implemented simultaneously with the 100 million financial public debt, but recently, there has been no further news. This matter is of great importance to national industry and commerce. Our association has separately telegraphed the Executive Yuan, the Legislative Yuan, the Ministry of Finance, and the Ministry of Industry, urging them to issue the order immediately to save the critical situation, and requesting your association to telegraph the various ministries and departments in Nanjing to urge them to issue the order immediately, so as to avoid any changes. We sincerely hope for this.

Upon arriving at the meeting, it was found that the current transit tax, the abolished inland half tax, and the re-import half tax are all domestic pass-through taxes in nature. According to the tariff systems of modern countries, they should not be retained. It was only because of the government's financial difficulties at the time, and the need to comprehensively plan the budget, that a gradual approach was necessary. Now, we are fortunate that your ministry understands the bleak market situation and has proposed a resolute abolition, which has been widely welcomed by merchants and residents, who are eagerly anticipating its implementation. The issue that is currently being considered is the problem of compensation. It is reported that the annual revenue from the transit tax is only 15 million. If a few import goods, either non-daily necessities or daily necessities that are in competition with domestic products, can be selected for appropriate increase in import tax to make up the shortfall, there should be no difference in government funds. Since your ministry has this proposal, it should already have a plan on how to make up the shortfall. We pray that you will finalize the plan and implement it as soon as possible, so that the commercial difficulties can be alleviated and everyone can feel the comfort of hope.

Shanghai Chamber of Commerce. Jiang.

Cotton and Textile Industries Follow Suit; Promoting Commercial Acceptance Drafts; Ke Ganchen and Zhu Wenqi Reply to Luo Qinghua, Having Submitted Proposals to Respective Trade Associations for Consensus and Implementation

Since the proposal for commercial acceptance drafts was put forward by Mr. Luo Qinghua, the chairman of the Silk and Satin Industry Association, it has been widely supported. The silk and satin industry and the electric silk weaving factory have already taken the lead in formally implementing it from April 1st, and it is progressing very smoothly. Luo Qinghua recently sent separate letters to Mr. Ke Ganchen, a leader in the cotton weaving industry, and Mr. Zhu Wenqi, a leader in the dyeing and weaving industry, requesting their support in promoting it. Ke and Luo have now replied, stating that they have submitted proposals to their respective trade associations for unanimous promotion, in order to alleviate the current difficulties. The original letters from the two gentlemen are transcribed as follows:

Zhu Wenqi's Letter

Zhu Wenqi's reply states that he received the letter, advocating commercial acceptance drafts, and believes that the financial panic in Shanghai is unprecedented. The reason is the large amount of import surplus and the large-scale export of silver. Commentators often say that promoting national products to reduce imports or the United States voluntarily abandoning its silver policy can end the panic. However, the first priority for imports is the food and cotton needed for our lives. In the present situation where rural construction has not yet been put on track, it is difficult to ensure its effectiveness. To expect the cessation of silver collection is even more like seeking skin from a tiger. At this most difficult time, we industrialists and businessmen must come up with a self-saving plan. The commercial acceptance drafts created by the teacher are a perfect and effective way to save ourselves. Your planning has benefited merchants greatly. In addition to submitting the proposal to our industry association for unanimous promotion, I hereby reply specially, wishing you peace. Your younger brother Zhu Zhiwenqi respectfully.

Ke Ganchen's Letter

Ke Ganchen's reply states that he received the letter yesterday, detailing the procedures for implementing acceptance drafts, and learned that your industry has already implemented it on April 1st, which shows your determination and is deeply admired. Acceptance drafts are popular in Europe and the United States and have been effective for a long time. Our country's business community has always adopted a credit-based system. As a result of years of import surplus and the impact of the US silver policy last year, silver and goods have flowed out, and the domestic currency has become scarce. In addition, rural areas are declining, and industries and businesses are going bankrupt. People are anxious and eager to remedy the situation. Although various parties have repeatedly called for relief and made many suggestions, the most self-saving, practical and easy to implement is your brother's implementation of acceptance drafts. With the progress of modern society, personnel affairs are becoming more complicated. Relying solely on the credit-based loans of the past is not enough to cope with the current environment. In a so-called capitalist society, the circulation of industrial securities is still needed. General businesses are afraid of extending credit and also suffer from the stagnation of debt collection, which affects the circulation of the economy. If acceptance drafts are implemented, they will transform stagnation into circulation and are a good medicine for the problem. However, there are two points to be studied: (1) Whether the various industries themselves can unite and be consistent in their actions and words; (2) Whether the money industry can do its best to cooperate and discount as much as possible. These still need our efforts to achieve the implementation of controlled trade, in order to ensure its success. With the enthusiastic promotion of your industry and the sincere support of the leaders in the financial community, your brother's call will surely be echoed by the masses. Eliminating abuses and benefiting others is not the job of strangers, and extraordinary achievements depend on your brother. Your younger brother will not hesitate to do his best to work together to promote progress. In addition to requesting the colleagues of my industry to agree, I also plan to convene a joint meeting of the Executive and Supervisory Committees immediately to discuss and decide on the implementation. I hope you will not hesitate to give us your guidance so that we can attach ourselves to your success. If there are any difficulties in the promotion, I hope you will show them so that we can try to overcome them together.

Respectfully, wishing you peace. Your younger brother Ke Ganchen respectfully.

Three Youths from America and Germany Set Sail Together, Hoping to Find Gold and Pearls

As previously reported, two American youths and one German youth plan to sail together on the Flying Dutchman from Shanghai to the vast ocean to seek sunken gold. The ship has already weighed anchor on Wednesday night (the 3rd of this month) and set sail for Songkou. If the weather is good, it will first go to the north coast of Taiwan on Thursday, then to Manila, and then to New Guinea. The three plan to first look for gold off the coast of the island. If they don't find anything, they plan to seek pearls off the north coast of Australia. If they still don't find anything, they plan to go around the Cape of Good Hope to the west coast of Africa to look for sunken gold in the sea. The ship is only 35 feet long, but the hull is very strong, and the navigation equipment is complete. The three youths are named Gates, Leet, and Roeping.

Chinese Man Killed by American Soldier Identified as Zhang Songxiang; Worked as a Servant in a Westerner's Home; Family Claimed the Body Yesterday

On the evening of the 1st of this month at approximately 9:00 PM, a drunken American sailor, arm in arm with a Russian dancer, was walking along Rue de la Sainte Famille in the French Concession and beat an unnamed male passerby for no reason, causing him to bleed from the nose and faint. He was sent to the hospital. Due to severe concussion, he died despite medical treatment. The body was reported to the Second Special Court, which sent personnel to verify the identity. The body was collected by the party. The sailor who caused the accident was sent by the French police to the commander's headquarters for interrogation. All of this was previously reported. It was not until yesterday that a man from Yangzhou, Zhang Deyuan (38 years old, residing at 243 Xinxin Lane, Rue du Pere Froc), went to the morgue to identify the deceased as his younger brother, Zhang Songxiang, 32 years old, who worked as a servant in a Westerner's home at No. 1 Jingan Villa, Jingan Temple Road. He has a wife and children. Today, he petitioned the court to claim the body for burial and is preparing to make representations.

Robbers Fighting with Police; Stray Bullet Kills a Rickshaw Puller; Accident on Rue Sibeixing; Jiang Xichang Died in Vain

At approximately 9:00 PM the night before last, robbers broke into the Mingjing Machinery Factory on Tiantong'an Road in Zhabei. A neighbor noticed and called the police to arrest them. Immediately, police whistles sounded in chaos. The robbers knew that things were not good and fled in all directions. The police tracked and arrested them. In desperation, the robbers opened fire to resist arrest. The police also opened fire in return, chasing them to Rue Sibeixing. A rickshaw puller, Jiang Xichang (41 years old, from Chongming), happened to be passing by pulling a rickshaw when he was hit in the chest by a stray bullet, damaging a vital organ. He immediately fell to the ground and died. Yesterday morning, the police station in charge ordered the local security chief, Yan Liugen, to report to the local court for an autopsy. In the afternoon, Prosecutor Zhang Zi was appointed and accompanied by Examiner Xuan Zhiming to the scene for verification. It was ordered that the body be coffined and investigated. The deceased left behind a wife and three children, all of whom depended on the deceased for their livelihood. Now that he has died tragically, they have lost their support. His wife's cries were tragic, and those who saw them were saddened.

Six-Year-Old Assault Case Adjudicated

Dai Aying, a man from Haimen who opened a pig slaughterhouse on Yuezhou Road, died in the autumn of 1927. His wife remarried his partner, Lu Shouchang. However, the partners from Haimen, Dong Chenggui and Xiang Dongsheng, were quite dissatisfied with this matter and made things difficult for them. They demanded money unsuccessfully, and the grudges deepened. At approximately 1:00 AM on the morning of September 20, 1929, they colluded with A Wu, Shen A Er, Wang Yougen, and others who were soldiers on the run, and A Wu opened fire near the intersection of Yuezhou Road and Zhaofeng Road, shooting at Lu Shouchang in an attempt to take his life. However, he did not hit a vital organ, and they fled in a panic. Hua Pu No. 2247 rushed to the scene after hearing the alarm and only found two shell casings. The injured person was sent to the hospital for treatment and was fortunately discharged shortly after suffering a slight bullet graze on his back. The case was reported to the Jiading Road police station, but the perpetrators could not be apprehended. Six years passed until Hua Tan Long, Shao Yingfan, and Gan Tan, Chen Jinsheng, and Li Yinmin, arrested Dong Chenggui on Zhoujiazui Road on the morning of the 20th of last month at 8:55 AM. Wang Yougen, a man from Pudong, was arrested by the Public Security Bureau for a theft case in the Chinese area and was brought back to the police station. Dong and Dong were escorted to the First Special District Court. Dong Chenggui admitted that A Wu fired the shot. Wang Yougen claimed that he was invited by Dong to fight at the time and only heard the sound of gunfire when they arrived at the scene, so he fled and did not actually do anything. He said that he was fooled by Dong and others. They were ordered to be detained pending sentencing. Yesterday morning, Judge Wu Zehan presided over the court and sentenced Dong Chenggui to six years in prison. The number of days of detention before the determination of the judgment shall be offset against the imprisonment at a rate of two days for one day. The shell casings were confiscated. Wang Yougen was found not guilty. Industrial and Commercial Bureau lawyer Li Zhishan requested that he be remanded in custody during the appeal period, and the court approved.

Village Woman's Affair and Pregnancy: Hundreds of Attempts at Abortion Lead to Tragic Death; Also Fearing Childbirth and Unable to Face People, She Resolves to Abort; A Medicinal Herb Inserted into Her Lower Body Proves Fatal

Wang Dou-shi, a woman from the northern countryside of Yangzhou, is currently twenty-eight years old. Her husband, surnamed Wang, earns a living farming in their village. She has three children with him. Due to the family's poverty, she left her children to be cared for by her husband and came to Shanghai three years ago to work as a servant, using her wages to supplement the household income. Recently, she has been employed as a servant in the home of a family surnamed *Mou* in Yuqing Lane on Wenzhou Road in the Public Concession of this city. Her employer calls her Wang Ma. Around the eleventh month of the lunar calendar last year, while getting water at the public stove at the entrance of the lane, she met Li Xiu-jian, a fellow villager who works as a back scrubber at the hot spring bathhouse on the corner of Yunnan Road and Avenue Edward VII. This year, he is twenty-four years old. The two took an immediate liking to each other, found each other compatible, and had a great sense of

"meeting each other too late."

Soon, they engaged in a physical relationship. However, Li already has a wife who is with him in Shanghai. After Li began his affair with Dou-shi, he sent his wife back to their hometown and lived with Dou-shi. Unexpectedly, after several secret rendezvous, Dou-shi became pregnant. Now, more than three months along, she deeply fears that if she carries the pregnancy to term, the affair will be exposed, and she will be unable to face her husband and family. After discussing it thoroughly with her lover, Li Xiu-jian, they decided to abort the pregnancy. She spent three *yuan* and purchased musk from a traditional Chinese medicine store, but after swallowing it, it had

absolutely no effect.

On the afternoon of the 28th of last month, Li accompanied her to the home of an elderly midwife, Li Wang-shi, a native of Nanjing, located at No. 6 Milu Road, Fangbang Bridge in the French Concession. They requested her to find a way to perform an abortion. The midwife demanded fifteen *yuan*. Li and Dou-shi did not haggle over the price, only seeking to terminate the pregnancy, so they paid the full amount. Dou-shi stayed overnight at the midwife's house. The next afternoon, the midwife first inserted a medicinal herb (called *duijiecao*, or "connecting grass") into Dou-shi's lower body, but it still had no effect. The midwife then went to Wanxiangchun Herbal Medicine Store at No. 155 Bair Road and spent 670 *wen* to purchase a dose of an ancient formula labor-inducing drug,

consisting of four herbs.

After returning and having Dou-shi swallow it, it finally worked on the afternoon of the 30th. A piece of flesh from Dou-shi's abdomen was expelled. On the 1st of this month, the midwife urged Li to come and take Dou-shi away. Because Li had not rented a house in Shanghai and had nowhere to settle, he sent Dou-shi to stay temporarily with a relative at No. 40 Hongrui Lane on Xinfulu to rest and recover. Unexpectedly, after this ordeal, Dou-shi's body weakened, and she suffered unbearable abdominal pain. At 10:45 AM on the 3rd, Li accompanied Dou-shi to the Huilv Hospital at No. 130 Avenue Avénue Road, claiming that she was suffering from a miscarriage due to pregnancy and requested treatment. The hospital admitted her. Subsequently, after Dr. Xu Daoheng examined Dou-shi's uterus, he suspected that

there was a foreign object

causing decay and an unbearable stench. He determined that it was not a miscarriage but definitely a result of an induced abortion. As per regulations, he reported it to the Xin Zha Gate Police Station in charge. Detective Li Shi-kun was dispatched and brought Li Xiu-jian, the lover who had accompanied Dou-shi to the hospital, to the police station. Under interrogation, Li confessed the truth. The police chief, noting that the crime scene was in the French Concession, ordered Detective Li to transfer Li Xiu-jian to the French Police Station to handle the case. After questioning by the French Police's Western Detective Yang Gaofuski Li, he dispatched detectives Zheng Long, Qi Deqing, and others to first arrest Li Wang-shi (68 years old this year), who had performed the abortion. After questioning, she also admitted to performing

the abortion without denying it.

She stated that the medicinal herb that was inserted was taken out when the fetus was expelled. The detectives then went to the Wanxiangchun Herbal Medicine Store to purchase the dose of labor-inducing medicine that Li Wang-shi bought for Wang Baoshi to take and brought it back to the police station to be tested and verified. Unexpectedly, Wang Dou-shi ultimately succumbed to her illness, and treatment proved ineffective. She died at 6:30 AM yesterday at Huilv Hospital. The hospital notified the French Police Station, and Detective Zhang Chunsheng was dispatched. Dr. Xu Daoheng issued a diagnosis certificate. The body was then transported to the Tongren Fuyuan Branch Hall Forensic Examination Office. The deceased's family members are still in

the Yangzhou countryside,

and there are no relatives in Shanghai. The French Police Station reported it to the Special District Court Procuratorate, which dispatched Prosecutor Wang Ren, along with forensic doctor Jiang Xuan and clerk Peng Xu, to the office to examine the body, take their official seats, and begin the official investigation. First, the Chinese and Western detectives reported the details of the case. Under questioning, Li Xiu-jian stated that he had known the deceased for only three months. Because she was pregnant, she told him she wanted an abortion. She found Li Wang-shi's residence herself and asked him to accompany her there. Three days later, he went to pick her up. Yesterday, he sent her to the hospital for treatment. Li Wang-shi stated that the deceased and Li came together and requested her to perform an abortion. She refused. She said she had taken three *yuan* worth of

musk, but it was ineffective.

She knelt down and begged her, so she agreed and only gave her labor-inducing medicine and did not insert any medicinal herbs. After verifying the confessions, Prosecutor Wang ruled that Wang Ma, also known as Wang Dou-shi, had indeed died due to the abortion. The body was handed over to Tongren Fuyuan Hall to be photographed, coffined, and buried. The diagnosis certificate and proof document were attached to the file. The defendants were taken into custody by the police department to be handled according to the law. After the ruling, Prosecutor Wang and Jiang De-fa, for the sake of caution, dissected the body and conducted a detailed examination. Because the body was offensively rancid, Tongren Fuyuan Hall issued a plank coffin to collect the body, which was transported to the burial ground this morning for burial, pending the arrival of the family members in Shanghai to claim the body. The two defendants, Li Xiu-jian and Wang Li-shi, were taken back to the police station by the patrol officers to be detained, pending their transfer to the Special District Court today for questioning.

Large Number of Robbers Arrested; Confiscated Jewelry and Firearms; Victim Testifies in Court; Identifies Robbers Present in Court

Huai Si Police Station Chinese Detective Shang Wu and patrolman Wang You-shan learned that a large gang of robbers was hiding at No. 621 Avenue Edward VII in the French Concession, plotting illegal activities. At 10:30 AM the day before yesterday, they, along with Western Detective Chief Gibbson and Chinese detectives, secretly went with the French Police's Chinese and Western detectives to the address and successively arrested Dong A-ping from Ningbo, Dong Mao-shi, Wang Xi-gen from Wuxi, Wang Zheng-lin from Yangzhou, Chuan Hai-zhou from Anhui, Li Hui-jun from Pinghu, Wang Shen-shi, and seven others. Items such as pearl necklaces, jewelry, and gold watches were confiscated. They then continued to the investigation at the entrance of the Gongping Hostel at Dongxin Bridge, where they apprehended fellow gang members Zhou Ji-min and Tong Chong-fa from Ningbo, and Wang San-bao, a woman from Suzhou. After taking all ten back to the police station for investigation, it was learned that these individuals were involved in the armed robbery of No. 23, Lane 153, Xiangjiazhui Road on October 17th of last year and the robbery of Yan Xiao-yong's home at No. 10, Lane 231, Qipu Road at noon on March 19th of this year. When questioned, all the defendants initially tried to deny it and refused to admit anything. Later, Tong Chong-fa confessed to participating in the robbery of Yan's house on Qipu Road with Dong A-ping, Wang Xi-gen, Kai Ji-min, and the fugitive Kuang A-liu, and others, and stated that there were firearms hidden at No. 172 Zhaojia Road in Nanshi. After obtaining this information, the Chinese and Western detectives again went with detectives from the Public Security Bureau to confiscate a leather suitcase containing four pistols, 216 bullets, five cartridge clips, a pair of binoculars, ten pieces of solid stone, two small silver ingots, two rings, two pairs of gold bracelets, one large gold fish bead, 21 small beads, as well as silver dollars, and other items. All of the items are stored in the Public Security Bureau, awaiting a formal request for transfer. Yesterday morning, the police station transferred the ten male suspects to the Eighth Criminal Court of the First Special District Court, requesting permission for detention to facilitate investigation. Zhang Tian-yin, the police station's lawyer, then stood up to present the case and submitted the confiscated items as evidence. Yan Xiao-yong, the victim from No. 10, Lane 232, Qipu Road, then filed a report stating that at noon on the 19th of last month, several robbers suddenly broke in. One robber, holding a gun, went upstairs and forced him to the back room downstairs to watch, then proceeded to rob the house. The three tenants, including himself, all suffered losses. He saw one robber holding a gun, who was the first defendant, Tong A-ping, and also identified the pearl necklace, watch, and crab-shaped gold brooch brought to the court by the police as items stolen from his home. Judge Liu Yugui verified the confessions, questioned each defendant, and ordered them to remain in custody pending further investigation at a later date.

Extortion Case; Suddenly Claims There Is Another Defendant; Clearly Agreed Upon After the Fact; Further Investigation Set for Later Date

Chen Guo-lin from Yancheng, because at 9 PM on the 26th of last month, he went to No. 66 Fulu Lane, Yangshupu Road, and attempted to extort twenty *yuan* from his fellow villager Lu Xiang-fang on some pretext. As a result, he obtained eight *yuan* by deception. Lu Xiang-fang's elder brother, Lu Xiang-qi, reported the incident to the Yangshupu Police Station. The arrest was unsuccessful until 11 AM the day before yesterday, when Chinese patrolman Hou Fu-lin checked his identity at the China Soap Factory and brought him to the police station for detention. Yesterday morning, he was transferred to the Third Criminal Court of the First District Court. Gong Bu Ju lawyer Li Zhi-shan stated that the case originated because the victim, Lu Xiang-fang, works at the Donghua Textile Factory during the day shift. Zhou, a Zhenjiang native, works the night shift at the same factory. His wife, Ren-shi, has a relationship with Lu Xiang-fang. The defendant learned of this. At the time, Lu and Ren-shi were whispering intimately in the room. The defendant broke in and said, "You are engaging in such improper behavior and must report it to the police. Pay twenty *yuan* to avoid trouble." Ren-shi, in desperation, broke off a piece of a gold bracelet and pawned it at the Changxing Pawnshop at No. 2174, on the same road, for eight *yuan*, which she handed over. Lu wrote an IOU for the remaining amount to be paid later. On the 28th, the defendant went again to demand payment. His brother, Lu Xiang-qi, learned of the details and, finding that the defendant lived at No. 40 in the same lane, reported it to the police station. He then fled, claiming he was trying to mediate a settlement. Yesterday at the police station, Lu Xiang-qi suddenly claimed that the defendant was not the person, but another Chen Gui-lin, who was taller, had a shaved head, and looked different. However, the age, height, and appearance that he had reported at the time were all consistent with Chen Guo-lin. Clearly, both sides had reached an agreement after the fact, and the defendant dared to go to the soap factory and work as usual after being arrested. The victim, Lu Xiang-fang, also failed to appear in court. Only his brother-in-law came to court. Lu Xiang-qi stated that there was another Chen Gui-lin living at No. 40 in the same lane as the defendant, who was currently on the run, and that the person currently in custody was indeed different in appearance and stature and could not be fingerprinted. Huang Ren-shi, however, claimed that she had no improper relationship with Lu Xiang-fang, that the defendant had not come to expose them at the time, and that the gold bracelet was borrowed by Lu. She gave evasive answers. The defendant stated that his name was Chen Guo-lin and that there was no Chen Gui-lin living with him. He had been living there for over a year and had not attempted to extort Lu Xiang-fang, firmly denying the charges. Judge Wu Ze-han ruled that he would remain in custody, and a further investigation would be scheduled to determine the facts.

Armed Robbery with Toy Gun; Two Robbers Sentenced to One Year and Nine Months Each

Pan Jin-qi and Lu Tao-sheng, natives of Songjiang, living in a flat in a private house on Guiyang Road, were originally carpenters. Recently, they were unemployed and living in poverty. At 9:15 PM on the 23rd of last month, they used a toy gun and an axe near a dark place, attempting to rob Cai Shao-qing, a native of Taizhou, of his property. The robbery was unsuccessful. Yangshupu Police Station Detective Liu Chang-gen arrested them, along with the weapons, and brought them to the police station, where they were sent to the First Special District Court for questioning and detention. Yesterday morning, Judge Jiang Shu-zhi continued the trial in court. Gong Bu Ju lawyer Li Zhi-shan stated that, after investigation, the two defendants had no other prior offenses and requested sentencing. Both Pan and Lu confessed that they were extremely impoverished, had no money to return home, and resorted to this desperate measure, begging for leniency. Judge Jiang sentenced Pan Jin-qi and Lu Tao-sheng each to one year and nine months in prison. The number of days of pre-trial detention will be deducted from the prison term at a rate of two days of detention equaling one day of imprisonment. The toy gun and axe were confiscated.

German World Cruise Ship "Lissauer" Sails North Yesterday Morning; President of American National Bank Also on Board Passing Through Shanghai

The German Hanjin Company's world cruise ship "Lissauer," carrying over 300 wealthy tourists from various countries, arrived in Shanghai the day before yesterday for sightseeing. It departed from the Gonghe Wharf in Hongkou at 8:00 AM yesterday morning to sail north to Qinhuangdao, and then travel to Beiping via the Beining Road for sightseeing. It is learned that among the passengers on the ship, in addition to nobles such as Prince and Princess von Hohenlohe-Langenburg and Prince and Princess zu Hohenlohe-Bartenstein, there are also Mr. and Mrs. Minikas, the president of the American National Bank, who also left Shanghai on the ship yesterday morning to travel north. The ship's tourists will stay in Beiping for three days, and then return to Qinhuangdao to board the original ship to Japan, and then through Hawaii, San Francisco, the Panama Canal, and other places. It is scheduled to return to New York on the 26th of next month.

First Bicycle Race Organized by the Road Association

The China National Road Construction Association, in order to raise public awareness of highway transportation and promote national physical training, is organizing the first bicycle riding competition, divided into men's, women's, and children's groups. The competition is scheduled for May 12th on Houlu Road behind the Shanghai Municipal Government. Registration has now begun. The competition rules are listed below: Article 1: This Association is holding a bicycle riding competition in order to raise public awareness of highway transportation and promote national physical training. Article 2: Any national of this country aged 16 or above, regardless of gender, may participate in the competition. A children's group is also established, limited to those under ten years of age. Article 3: The first competition is divided into three groups: A. Men's Group (40 kilometers), B. Women's Group (10 kilometers), C. Children's Group (1 kilometer). Each group has a quota of 50 participants. Article 4: Those who join the competition must personally go to the Association's headquarters at No. 70 Guzhao Road before April 20th (except Sundays) between 9:00 AM and 11:30 AM or between 2:00 PM and 5:00 PM to fill out the application form and guarantee form. The Association will then issue the competition rules and competition number plate. Article 5: Participants must pay a registration fee of one yuan at the time of registration. Once registered, it will not be refunded for any reason. The competition number plate must not be transferred to others, otherwise their right to compete will be canceled. Article 6: The competition location is Houlu Road behind the Shanghai Municipal Government. Article 7: The competition date is set for May 12th. It may be postponed for one week in case of rain. The competition time is scheduled to start at 9:00 AM. Article 8: The first competition will have one chief referee, one chief commander, two deputy commanders, and several judges, inspectors, and lap counters, who will be hired by the Association. Article 9: After the competition is completed, the chief referee will judge the results, and prizes will be awarded according to the level of excellence, limited to the top three in each group. Article 10: These rules will be implemented after review by the Executive Board of the Association. The competition regulations will be determined separately.

Since the beginning of spring, thefts have repeatedly occurred in Sanlintang Town, Pudong, Shanghai County. New Pharmaceutical Industry Association Notifies: Starting Today, Members Will Be Dispatched to Investigate Whether Colleagues are Complying with Industry Regulations

The New Pharmaceutical Industry Association has decided to dispatch members starting today to investigate whether colleagues are complying with industry regulations. The following announcement was issued yesterday: To Whom It May Concern: The industry regulations set by this Association and the No. 1 retail price list agreed upon by the Evaluation Committee are scheduled to take effect on April 1st and have already been published in the newspaper and announced. At the same time, they have been reported to the Shanghai Municipal Social Bureau for record. All fifteen evaluation committee members have been divided into three groups to handle investigation matters, with each group serving for one month on a rotating basis. Group 1: Central, Huamei, Tianhua, Sino-French, Zhengwei; Group 2: Wuzhou, Jicheng, Wanguo, Sino-Western, Huayang; Group 3: Jihuatang, Dahua, Dazhong, Yong'an, Nanyang. The Association has prepared investigation certificates for distribution and use to show solemnity. The investigation methods are listed as follows: (1) Preliminary investigation: The investigating group on duty for the month will handle it themselves. (2) Each member of the investigating group must have an investigation report when the group rotates each month. (3) If someone discovers that a certain pharmacy is not complying with the publicly agreed-upon price, they should notify the investigating group on duty for the month. After receiving the report, the group will immediately notify each other so that they can jointly hold certificates and go to the site for investigation. The investigation matters for this month will be undertaken by Group 1, starting on the 5th. They plan to start the investigation with certificates. When they arrive at your location, please assist in the process. The matter concerns the interests of all colleagues in the industry and must be uniformly observed to uphold the law. Sincerely. To a certain major pharmacy.

Recent News from the Pudong Native Association: Hanxing Wins Water and Electricity Project Bid

Since the Pudong Native Association began construction of its new clubhouse last year, the project has progressed quite rapidly. All the foundation pits have been completed. Bids were also invited for the internal water and electricity projects. The bidding was held at 2:00 PM on April 2nd at the association. There were ten bidders for the electrical work. The highest bids, from Hengsheng and Ruihua, were above 74,000 yuan. The bids between 50,000 and 60,000 yuan came from Langji, Jinda, Jie, Xinghua, Huiying, Hejiang, and Rongde. Hanxing's bid was the lowest at 4,981 yuan, and the remaining bids were between 5,000 and 6,000 yuan. Yesterday afternoon, the association's Construction Special Committee jointly decided at the Du residence to award the contract to Hanxing, the lowest bidder. The total cost of the water and electricity projects is 49,525 yuan.

4th Railway Exhibition; Qingdao Sales Office Increases Booth Space; Ministry of Railways Approves Additional 50 Booths

In recent years, the Ministry of Railways has held national railway line product exhibitions and set up sales offices to promote the development and sale of domestic goods. The original purpose was to increase the effectiveness of the exhibition and promote domestic products on the ground. This time, it is planned to hold the 4th Railway Exhibition in Qingdao. Since the start of registration, manufacturers from all over the country have actively participated, and the quota has been filled. As a result, those who arrived late could not participate. The Joint Association of Domestic Goods Manufacturers along the Beijing-Shanghai and Shanghai-Hangzhou-Ningbo Railways, in view of the fact that the Ministry of Railways stipulated that the number of manufacturers along the Beijing-Shanghai and Hangzhou-Yong Railways participating was too small and the booth space was insufficient, and that many of the large factories of the association's members were left out due to the quota being filled, specially telegraphed the Ministry of Railways to increase the booth space by 50 booths to facilitate them and show universality and so on. According to the Ministry of Railways' reply yesterday, the manufacturers of the association have a special relationship with the railway side, and it should be approved to increase the booth space by 50 booths to show special accommodation. The two railway administrations will be notified to handle this matter. The association's office is located at 602 Fengjili, Guizhou Road. The manufacturers in this city who go there to register and participate are very enthusiastic.

Telegraph Bureau Expands Scope of Accepting and Sending Social Telegrams

The Ministry of Communications recently issued an order to all telegraph bureaus and stations that, starting from April 1st, all telegrams concerning (A) congratulations on the New Year, weddings, birth of children, birthdays, anniversaries, graduations, going abroad, opening ceremonies, moving, passing exams, promotions, taking office, successful inventions, victories, ceremonies, awards; (B) condolences for death and burial; (C) condolences for illness, disaster, carelessness, injury, theft, failure; (D) expressions of welcome and farewell and reply telegrams should be accepted and sent as social telegrams. The Shanghai Telegraph Bureau on Sichuan Road in this city has received this order and has notified all post offices and telegraph offices to comply.

Zhabei Affected by the Completion of the Wusong River Dredging; Yellow Panic Occurs; Manure Boats Cannot Export Due to Traffic Obstruction; Cleaning Workers Jointly Petition the Authorities

Since the Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Commission built dams at Yujidun and other places to dredge the Wusong River, manure boats have been affected by traffic, causing an unprecedented yellow panic in Zhabei. The city's cleaning workers petitioned the authorities again yesterday to oppose the ban on collecting fees. Details are recorded below:

Completion Affects Boat Traffic

The Taihu Lake Water Conservancy Commission built dams at Yujidun and other places to dredge the Wusong River, cutting off traffic. Rice boats in North Shanghai were the first to be affected and had to detour through the outer Huangpu River. However, manure boats in Zhabei are usually purchased daily by farmers from Huangdu, Qingpu, Zhujiajiao, and other places in small boats. These small boats are not convenient for detouring through the outer Huangpu River. Now, affected by the broken dam, Zhabei manure cannot be exported, causing an unprecedented yellow panic. The Zhabei Cleaning Workers' Union has submitted a request to the Finance and Health Bureaus, urging them to find a solution as soon as possible.

Occupations Petition to Allow Fee Collection

Since the An Gong Society and the Health Bureau jointly announced in February that manure collectors would be banned from collecting monthly fees from residents, cleaning workers in various districts of Shanghai, including South Shanghai, North Shanghai, and Hongkou, have relied on the wine money given by users as their only income. The authorities have not formulated a relief plan, but instead banned them, affecting the workers' livelihoods. They have repeatedly petitioned the authorities, but without result. Yesterday, cleaning workers' unions from the first district (South Shanghai), the fourth district (Hongkou), the seventh district (Xiangyan Bridge), and the sixth district (Zhabei) specially sent representatives to the city party headquarters to petition for relief. The authorities promised to reply with concrete measures on the 6th.

Delayed Wage Payment Causes Dispute

There are more than 200 cleaning workers in Zhabei District, who are employed by the Zhabei Cleaning Office. Each worker's wage is at most 8.5 yuan per month. According to the usual practice, each person can borrow 3 yuan on the 16th of each month, and the rest is paid off on the 4th of the following month. The cleaning office has delayed paying this month's wages, so all the workers are panicked. Representatives were sent to negotiate, but there was no result. The cleaning office said that the ships have been blocked by traffic in recent days, the exports have been cut off, and the business is light. It promised to pay the arrears on the 10th. However, the workers (1) believe that their income will be sharply reduced during the period when ships are cut off, and (2) are panicked about their lives, so they all expressed opposition and planned to request the authorities to find a way to provide relief.

The Truth of the Murder Case on Haichang Road: It Turns Out to Be an Affair; The Son's Detailed Confession

On the evening of the 2nd of this month, at about 7:00 PM, the house of Yang Wenxiang, located at 18 Ruyi Lane, Haichang Road, Zhabei, was attacked by thugs who fired a volley of bullets, killing Yang's wife and daughter, as well as four of the thugs. This was reported in the newspapers. It is now known that after the case occurred, Ruan Kaiji, the director of the Xinzha Sub-bureau, summoned Yu Zhu, the second landlord of the house, and Kou Dizi, the young daughter of the deceased Yang Ji. Yu Zhu confessed that she was 47 years old and from Pudong. My husband is in a small business and is not often at home. I live in the front building, and Yang Wenxiang lives in the back building and the pavilion. There is a reception room downstairs in the back that is rented to someone who makes leather boxes. The day before yesterday evening, I was washing dishes in my room when I suddenly heard the sound of gunfire. I was so scared that I shrank into a ball. After the gunfire stopped, I heard Yang Wenxiang's young daughter Kou Dizi shout that someone was killed. I crawled out and saw Yang Wenxiang's wife, his eldest daughter Kouzi, and a man, all lying dead in a pool of blood on the floor. I don't know if the man usually came to his house or not, but yesterday (that is, the day before) I heard Yang Ji scolding her eldest daughter Kouzi, and the man didn't allow her to scold her. Kou Dizi confessed that she was 15 years old. The day before yesterday evening, Sun Jingyu (referring to the thug) came to my house. My mother scolded my sister, and Sun didn't allow my mother to scold her. At that time, I was standing next to my mother, and my sister was standing opposite. When the Sun surname saw that my mother didn't listen to him, he shot my mother. After my sister was killed, he killed himself, and I dared to come out. The Sun surname often came to my house, and was in love with my sister. My mother knew about it, and because she didn't want it, she told my sister not to be with the Sun surname. Yang Wenxiang confessed that he was 43 years old and that he shaved heads at the Shanghai Bank. He went out at 6:00 AM every day and came back at 7:00 or 8:00 PM, so he didn't know anything about the affairs at home. He only found out about what happened last night after his young daughter and neighbors told him. After the examiner Wang Chongren verified the confession, he determined that the case was indeed caused by Sun Jingyu, who killed Yang Ji because she prevented her eldest daughter Yang Kouzi from having an affair with the Sun surname. Sun had already committed suicide, so the details of the interrogation were reported to the general bureau for investigation. It is also known that the body of the thug was collected by the local security guard yesterday. The husband of the deceased Yang Ji was also summoned to the Shanghai Local Court for questioning yesterday.

After the Robbery Case on Qipu Road Was Solved, Feng Xiangbing Was Actually Encountered on the Road

Ge Bosen, a Western detective from the Public Concession Huishi Police Station, and Shang Wu, a Chinese detective, captured seven habitual thieves who robbed a family surnamed in Qipu Road No. 10. Zhou arranged for transportation, and returned them after use. The Chinese and Western detectives secretly went to the house with the Public Security Bureau the night before, but Feng was not at home. Zhou identified him, and four pistols and two hundred and sixteen bullets (yesterday's newspaper mistakenly wrote one hundred and sixteen bullets) and stolen goods were seized. This was reported in yesterday's newspaper. Liu Yunfang, the police chief in charge, considered that there were bandits hiding in his jurisdiction and privately hiding a large number of weapons, which was extremely bold and reckless. Second Special Court Reduces Salaries

The Shanghai Second Special District Local Court and the Jiangsu High Court Third Branch have recently reduced salaries for March due to financial difficulties. Except for employees whose salaries are less than 100 yuan, which are still paid as before, the remaining employees are paid 70% for those with salaries of 100 yuan or more, 65% for those with salaries of 300 yuan or more, and 60% for those with salaries of 400 yuan or more. It is reported that this salary reduction is unprecedented since the national crisis. Although the judicial income of the court is less than that of the First Special District, the number of lawsuits has increased greatly, especially civil cases. Judging from the income and expenditure of the local court, the income and expenditure can still offset each other. The total deficit of the high and local courts is also very limited. However, because the Second Special District Prison was taken back, the monthly expenses are burdened with more than 17,000 yuan, and the detention center also needs 3,000 yuan. Therefore, the deficit is very large. Although the Ministry of Judicial Administration still subsidizes 20,000 yuan per month, it is only enough to offset the expenses of the prison and detention center. As a result, the employees of the two courts are all complaining.

Qianli Steamer Aground in the Huangpu River After Flooding

The Qianli steamer of Zhengji Steamship Company was damaged in the Huangpu River yesterday morning. The hull was broken and flooded. The ship has now run aground for rescue and is ready for major repairs at the factory. The details are as follows:

Empty Boat Floods

The Qianli steamer of Zhengji Company is the company's largest steamer, with a load capacity of 2,913 tons. It originally sailed to Dalian, Tianjin, Qingdao, Shanghai, and various ports in South China. This time, it arrived in Shanghai from North China and unloaded its cargo. It was scheduled to sail empty to Qingdao yesterday morning to load coal. At 5:10 AM yesterday morning, the Qianli steamer sailed from Shanghai. Unexpectedly, when it reached the Huangpu River in front of the Zhabei Hydropower Plant in the Wusongkou, the bow of the Qianli steamer suddenly sank into the river. The shipowner was informed and immediately went to the bow to inspect. He saw that the bow had been flooded to six feet in a short time, and the situation was very dangerous.

Self-Grounding

At this time, the shipowner was very frightened and did not know the cause of the flooding in the bow. Seeing the bow sinking, he was deeply concerned about the occurrence of major dangers. In order to seek rescue, he immediately drove the Qianli steamer to the shallow beach near the Zhabei Hydropower Plant and made it ground itself to avoid the danger of the hull being flooded. At the same time, the shipowner sent someone to report to the company on Tianzhutang Street and reported to the Maritime Bureau and the Insurance Federation to send someone to inspect the ship.

Verifying Damage

At noon, Zhengji Company received this report and immediately reported it to the Maritime Bureau and the Insurance Federation according to the shipowner's report and asked ship inspector Cao Shulian to go to the vicinity of the Zhabei Hydropower Plant to inspect the ship. By the afternoon, Mr. Cao had verified that there was a hole on the left side of the bottom of the bow compartment of Qianli, which was three inches long and half an inch wide. River water entered from here. It is not known when the hole was broken. The company has now decided to temporarily use a plugging method to fill the hole in the bottom of the ship, and then pump out the water and tow it out of the shallows.

Factory Repair

After the Qianli accident, Zhengji Company immediately telegraphed its Yantai head office and notified the Qingdao branch. When a reporter from this newspaper inquired at the company, Mr. Liang of the company said that the shipowner did not know how the Qianli was damaged. Fortunately, it was discovered in the Huangpu River, so it was easy to repair. It has now been decided to fill the hole in the bottom of the ship and then tow it into the shipyard for repairs.

Killed for One Yuan; Two Fists Cannot Beat Four Hands; Qu Fuqing Died at the Hands of Two Gaos

Qu Fuqing (52 years old), a native of Liuhe, Pudong, who lived at 52 Huayuan Shiqiao Road, had two small cars for rent. Gao Jianglang and Gao Xiaogou, two brothers from Chongming who lived across the street, rented a car from Qu for one yuan a month. By the end of last month, they owed six yuan in rent, which had not been paid for a long time. Recently, they also reported that the car was lost. At 9:30 PM the night before last, Qu Fuqing asked Gao Jianglang for the car rent again. The Gao brothers not only refused to pay, but also spoke rudely. So a quarrel broke out. Gao Jianglang rushed forward, twisted Qu and beat him. Gao Xiaogou also helped his brother press Qu down and punched him hard. Qu was old after all, and two fists could not beat four hands. He was beaten and injured. At that time, people persuaded them to disperse. Unexpectedly, after Qu Fuqing returned home, he held his lower abdomen with both hands and called out in pain. He died at 1:00 AM that night. His wife reported to the police station, and the police were sent to arrest him. The culprits had already fled after hearing the news. Yesterday morning, the local security guard Lu Shunlong reported to the local court to request an autopsy. The order was to wait for someone to be sent for the autopsy.

Three Suicide Attempts by Poisoning

Zhao Yunshan, about twenty years old, who ran a printing business at No. 126, Yanqing Lane, Guizhou Road, in a street-facing pavilion room, and his wife, Ms. Chen, about eighteen years old, contemplated suicide due to financial difficulties yesterday. The couple simultaneously ingested raw opium. Neighbors noticed and rushed them to Renji Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the rescue was timely, and they were saved. At the Oriental Hotel on Xizang Road, around 9 PM the night before, a Western-dressed traveler, claiming to be Wang Chunlin, a local of thirty years old, booked room 596. Somehow, he secretly swallowed a large amount of opium at midnight. The room attendant discovered him unconscious and reported to the front desk, who then reported to the Old North Station Police. Detectives arrived and summoned an ambulance to take him to Renji Hospital. It was said that he had taken an overdose of poison, and his life was in danger.

Chen Hongqing, a traveler from Ningbo, about thirty years old, was in room 210 of the Ningbo Merchant Hotel at No. 296 Tianjin Road. Due to prolonged unemployment and inability to make a living, he contemplated suicide. He wrote a suicide note and swallowed poison after 10 PM last night. The room attendant discovered him and reported to the nearby Old Zha Police Station, who sent detective No. 339 to take him to Renji Hospital.
